Kiṃchañanda pātakaṃ  Kiṃ chando kimadhippāyo eko sammasi ghammaniKiṃ patthayāno kiṃ esaṃ kena atthena brāhmaṇa  Yathā mahāvāridharo kumbho suparinābhavāTathupamaṃ ambapakkaṃ vaṇṇagandharasuttamaṃ Taṃ vuyhamānaṃ sotena disvānāmalamajjhimePāṇihi naṃ gahetvāna agyāyatanamāhariṃ Tato kadalipattesu nikkhipitvā sayaṃ abhaṃSatthena na ṃvikappetvā khuppipāsaṃ ahāsi me Sohaṃ apetadaratho vyantibhuto dukhakkhamo Assādaṃ nādhigacchāmi phalesavaññesu kesupi Sosetvā  nūna maraṇaṃ taṃ mamaṃ āvahisastiAmbaṃ yassa phalaṃ sāduṃ madhuraggaṃ manoramaṃYamuddhariṃ vuyhamānaṃ udadhismā mahaṇṇave Akkhātaṃ te mayā sabbaṃ yasmā upavasāmahaṃRammaṃ patinisinnosmi puthulomāyutā puthu Tvaṃ ca kho me akkhāsi attānamapalāyinīKā vā tvamasi kalyāṇi kissa vā tvaṃ sumajjhime Ruppapaṭṭapaḷimaṭṭhava vyagghiva girisānujāYā sanni nāriyo devesu devānaṃ paricārikā Yāva manussalokasmiṃ rūpenatvāgatiyoRūpe te sādisi natthi devesu gandhabbamanussaloke Phuṭaṭhāsi me cārupubbaṅgi brūhiAkkhāhi me nāmañca bandhave ca   Yaṃ tvaṃ patinisinnosi rammaṃ brāhmaṇa kosikiṃSāhaṃ bhusālayāvutthā varavārivahoghasā Nānādumaṇākiṇṇā bahutā girikandarāMameva pamukhā honti abhisandanti pāvuse Dakkha  machasaṃ syā  Sesitvā  machasaṃ syā Devagandhabbamānuse  syā  Brūhi nāmañca bandhave  syā   Atho bahu vanā todā nilavārivahandharāBahukā nāgacittodā abhisandanti vārinā Tā ambajambulabujā nipā tālā cudumbarā Bahuni phalajātāni āvahanti abhiṇhaso Yaṃ kiñci ubhato tīre phalaṃ patati ambuniAsaṃsayaṃ taṃ sotassa phalaṃ hoti vasānugaṃ Etadaññāya medhāvi puthupañña suṇohi meMā rocayamabhisaṅgaṃ paṭisedha janādhipa Na cāhaṃ vaddhavaṃ maññe yaṃ tvaṃ raṭṭhābhivaddhanaĀceyyamāno rājisi maraṇaṃ abhikaṅkasi Tassa jānanti pitaro gandhabbā ca sadevakāYe cāpi isayo loke saññatattā yasassino Asaṃsayante  jānanti vaddhabhūtā yasassino  Evaṃ viditvā vidu sabbadhammaṃViddhaṃsanaṃ cavanaṃ jīvitassaNāciyati tassa narassa pāpaṃSace na ceteti vadhāya tassa Isipugasamaññāte evaṃ lokyā vaditā satiAnariya  parisambhāse pāpakammaṃ jigiṃsasi  Sace ahaṃ marissāmi tīre te puthu susesāṇiAsaṃsayaṃ asiloko mayi pete āgamissati Tasmā hi pāpakaṃ kammaṃ rakkhasve  sumajjhimeMā taṃ  sabbo jano pacchā pakatthāsi mayi mate  Aññātametaṃ avisayhasāhiAttānaṃ ambaṃ ca dadāmi te taṃYo duccaje kāmaguṇe pahāyaSantiñca dhammañca adiṭṭhitosi Nipā tālamudumbarā  machasaṃ  Jigisasi  machasaṃ Tapassino  machasaṃ  Rakkhassuva  syā Asaṃsayaṃ tepi  machasaṃ  Tvaṃ  syā Anariyaṃ  vi syā  Yo hitvā pubbasaṃyogaṃ pacchā saṃyojane ṭhitoAdhammañcava carati pāpañcassa pavaḍḍhati Ehi taṃ pāpayissāmi kāmaṃ appossukko bhavaUpānayāmi sitasmiṃ viharāhi anussuko Taṃ pupparasamattehi vakkaṅgehi arindamaKoñca mayurā diviyā koyaṭṭhimadhusāliyā Kujitā haṃsapugehi kokilettha pabodhareAmbettha vippasunaggā palālakhapasannibhāAkosumbhasalalā nīpā pakkatālavilambīno  Mālī tiriṭī kāyuri aṅgadi candanassadoRattiṃ tvaṃ paricāresi divā vedesi cedanaṃ Soḷasitthisahassāni yā temā paricārikāEvaṃ mahānubhāvosi abbhuto lomahaṃsano Kiṃ kammavakari pubbe pāpaṃ attadukhāvahaṃYaṃ karitvā manussesu paṭṭhimaṃsāni khādasi  Ajjhenāni paṭiggayha kāmesu gathito ahaṃAcariṃ dighamaddhānaṃ paresaṃ ahitāyahaṃ Yo piṭṭhimaṃsiko hoti evaṃ ukkacca khādatiYathāhamajja khādāmi piṭṭhimaṃsāni attanotiKiṃchanda jātakaṃ  Kumbajātakaṃ  Ko pāturāsi tidivā nabhambhiObāsayaṃ saṃvariṃ candimāvaGattehi te rasmiyo niccharantiSateritā  vijjurivantalikkhe So chinnavātaṃ kamasi  aghambhiVehāsayaṃ gaccasi tiṭṭhasi caIddhi nu te vatthukatā subhāvitāAnaddhaguṇamapi devatānaṃ Vehāsayaṃ kamamāgamma tiṭṭhasi Kumbhaṃ kiṇāthāti yametamatthaṃKo vā tuvaṃ kissa vatāya kumbhoAkkhāhi me brāhmaṇa etamatthaṃ  Na sappikumbho napi telakumbhoNa phāṇitassa na madhussa kumbhoKumbhassa vajjāni anappakāniDose bahu kumbhagate suṇātha Galeyya yaṃ pitvā pate papātaṃSobbhaṃ guhaṃ candaniyoḷigallaṃBahumpi bhuñejayya abhojaneyyaṃTasasā puṇṇaṃ kumbamimaṃ kiṇātha  Yaṃ ve pitvā  cittasmiṃ  anesamānoĀbhiṇḍati goriva bhakkhasādiAnāthamāno upagāyati naccati caTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Yaṃ ve pitvā acelakova naggoCareyya gāme visikhantarāniSammuḷhacitto ativelasāyi Tassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Yaṃ ve pitvā vuṭṭhāya pavedhamānoSisañca bāhuñca pasārayantoSo naccati dārukaṭallakovaTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Sateratā  vi  Kappasi  Vehāsayaṃgammamāgamma tiṭaṭhasi  machasi Yaṃ pitvā  vi machasaṃ syā  Cittasmi  machasaṃ ativelacāritipi pāṭho  Yaṃ ve pitvā  aggidaḍḍhā sayantiAtho sigālehipi khāditāseBandhaṃ vadhaṃ bhogajāniñcupentiTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Yaṃ ve pitvā bhāseyya abhāsaneyyaṃSahāyamāsino apetavatthoSammakkhito vantagato vyasantoTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Yaṃ ve pitvā ukkaṭṭho āvilakkho Mameva sabbapaṭhavīti  maññatiNa me samo samo cāturanetāpi rājāTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Mānātimānā kalahāti pesuniDubbaṇṇini nanaggiyini palāyiniCorāna dhuttāna gati niketoTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Dhaññaṃ dhanaṃ rajataṃ jātarūpaṃKhettaṃ gavaṃ yattha vināsayantiUcchedani vittavataṃ kulānaṃTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Iddhāni phitāni kulāni asasuAnekasāhassadhanāni lokeUcchinnadāyajjakatānimāyaTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha  Yaṃ pitvā duṭṭharūpova posoAkkosati pitaraṃ mātarañcaSassumpi gaṇheyya athopi suṇhaṃTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Yaṃ ve pitvā duṭṭha  rūpāva nāriAkkosati sasuraṃ sāmikañcaDāsampi gaṇhe paricārakampiTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Pivitvā  machasaṃ syā  Atavelavāri tipi pāṭho Sabbāpaṭhaviti pi pāṭho  Corānaṃ dhuttānaṃ  vi machasaṃ  Ditta  vi machasaṃ  Yaṃ ve pivitvāna  bhaneyya posoDhamme ṭhitaṃ samaṇaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vāGacche apāyampi tato nidānaṃTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Yaṃ ve pitvā duccaritaṃ carantiKāyena vācāya ca cetasā vāNirayaṃ vajanti duccaritaṃ caritvāTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Yaṃ yācamānā na labhanti pubbeBahuṃ hiraññampi pariccajantāSo taṃ pivitvā alikaṃ bhaṇātiTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Yaṃ ve pitvā pesane pesayantoAccayike karaṇiyambhi jateAtthampi so nappajānāti vuttoTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Hirimanāpi ahirikabhāvaṃPātuṃ karonti madanāya mattāDhirāpi santā bahukaṃ bhaṇantiTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Yaṃ ve pitvā ekathupā sayantiAnāsakā thaṇaḍiladukkhaseyyaṃDubbaṇiṇiyaṃ āyasakyañcupentiTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha  Yaṃ ve pitvā pattakkhandhā sayantiGāvo kuṭatārivaNahi vāruṇiyā vegoNarena sussahoriva Yaṃ manussā vivajjenti  sappaṃ ghoravisammivaTaṃ loke visasamānaṃ ko naro pātāmarahati Yaṃ ve pitvā andhakaveṇhuputtāSamuddatire piricārayantāUpakkamuṃ musalehaññamaññaṃTassā puṇaṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha Pitvāna  syā  Vivajjanti  machasaṃ  Yaṃ ve pitvā pubbadevā pamantāTidivā cutā sassatiyā samāyāTaṃ tādisaṃ majjamimaṃ niratthakaṃJānaṃ mahārāja kathaṃ pibeyya Nayimasmiṃ kumbasmiṃ dadhi vā madhuṃ vāEvaṃ abhiññāya kiṇāhi rājaAkkhātarūpaṃ tava sabbamitta  Na me pitā vā athavāpi mātāEtādiso yādisako tuvaṃsiHitānukampi paramatthakāmoSohaṃ karissaṃ vacanaṃ tavajja Dadāmi te gāmacarāni pañcaDāsisataṃ santa gavaṃ satāniĀjaññayutte ca rathe dasā imeĀcariyo hosi mamatthakāmo Taveva dāsi satamatthu rājaGāmā ca gāvo ca taveva hontuĀjaññayuttā ca rathā tavevaSakko hamasmi  tidasānamindo Maṃsodanaṃ sappipāyañca  bhuñjaKhādassu ca tvaṃ madhumāsapuve Evaṃ tuvaṃ dhammarato janindaAnindito saggamupehi ṭhānantiKambhajātakaṃ Jayaddisajātakaṃ  Cirassaṃ vata me adapādi ājjaBhakkho mahā sattamibhattakāleKutosi ko vāsi tadiṅgha brūhiĀcikkha jātiṃ vidito yathāpi Hamasmiṃ  simu  Sappipāyāsa  vi machasaṃ  Madhunāsapupe  vi machasaṃ      Pañcālarājā migavaṃ paviṭṭho Jayaddiso nāma yadissuto teCarāmi kacchāni canāni cāhaṃPasadimaṃ  khāda mamajja muñca  Seneva tvaṃ paṇasi sassamāne Mameso bhakkho pasado yaṃ vadesiTaṃ khādiyāna pasadaṃ jighañakaññaṃKhādissaṃ pacchā na vilāpakālo Na catthi mokkho mama vikkayena Gantvāna pacchā gamanāyapaṇheTaṃ saṅgaraṃ brāhmaṇasasappadāyaSaccānurakkhi punarāvajissaṃ Kiṃ kammajātaṃ anutappati taṃ Pattaṃ samipaṃ maraṇassa rājaĀcikkha me taṃ api sakkuṇemuAnujānituṃ āgamanāya paṇhe  Katā mayā brāhmaṇassa dhanāsāTaṃ saṅgaraṃ paṭimokkhaṃ  na mutataṃTaṃ saṅgaraṃ brāhmaṇassappadāyaSaccānurakkhi punarāvajissaṃ Yaṃ te katā brāhmaṇassa dhanāsāTaṃ saṅgaraṃ paṭimokkhaṃ na muttaṃTaṃ saṃgaraṃ brāhmaṇassapapadāyaSaccānurakkhi punarāvajassu  Mutto ca so purisādassasahatthāGantvā sakaṃ mandiraṃ kāmakāmiTaṃ saṅgaraṃ brāhmaṇassappadāyaĀmantayi putta malinasattaṃ  Ajjeva rajjaṃ abhisecayassuDhammañca raṭṭhesu janesu cāpi Adhammakāro ca te māhu raṭṭheGacchāmahaṃ porisādasasa ñatte Pavuttho  vi  Pasadaṃ imaṃ  vi Sayhamāno  vi machasaṃ syā jighacchanti bhavitabba Nikkayena  machasaṃ syā  Anutappetvaṃ  machasaṃ Paṭimukkaṃ  machasaṃ  Malinasattuṃ  vi machasaṃ syā Dhammaṃ carassu puresucāpi  ma dhammaṃcaresesu paresu  machasaṃ  Kiṃ kamma kubbaṃ tava deva pādeNārādhayiṃ tadicchāmi sotuṃYamajja rajjambhi udasasaye tvaṃRajjampi na iccheyyaṃ  tayā vinā ahaṃ Na kamamunā vā vacasāva tātaAparādhitohaṃ tuviyaṃ sārāmiSandhiñca katvā purisādakenaSaccānurakkhi punahaṃ gamissaṃ  Ahaṃ gamissāmi idheva hohiNatthi tato jivato vippamokkhoSace tuvaṃ gacchasiyeva rājaAhmapi gacchāmi ubho na homa Addhā hi tāta satānesa dhammoMaraṇā ca me dukkhataraṃ tadasasaKammāsapādo taṃ yadā pacitvāPasayha khāde bhidā rukkha  sule Paṇena te pāṇamahaṃ nimissaṃMā tvamagā porisādasasa ñatteEtañca te pāṇamhaṃ nimissaṃTasmā mataṃ jīvitassa varemi   Tato bhave dhitimā rājaputtoVandittha mātucca pitucaca pādeDukhinissa mātā nipati pathabyā Pitassa paggayha bhujāni kandati Taṃ gacchantaṃ tāva pitā viditvāParammukho vandati pañajaliko Somo ca rājā varuṇo ca rājāPajāpati candimā suriyo caEtehi gutto purisādakambhāAnuññāto sotthi pachi tāta  Yaṃ daṇḍakāraññagatassa mātāMossakā  sotthānaṃ suguttāTante ahaṃ sotthānaṃ karomi etena saccena sarantu devāAnuñanaññāto sotthi paccehi putta Niccheyya  machasaṃ  Bhidarukkha  machasaṃ Vaṇṇemi  vi machasaṃ syā  Nipātāpathabyā vi  pathavyā  machasaṃ Pañjaliso  vi pañjalisā  maichasi  Rāmassakāsi  machasaṃ  Āvī raho vāpi manopadosaṃNāhaṃ sare jātumalinasatteEtena saccena sarantu devaAnuññāto sotthi paccehi hāta Yasmā ca me anadhimanosi sāmiNacāpi me manāsa appiyosiEtena saccena sarantu devāAnunaññāto sotthi pacecahi devā  Brahā uju cārumukho kutosiNa maṃ pajānāsi vane vasantaṃLuddañca maṃ ñatvā purisādakotiKo sotthimājānamidhāvajeyya Jānāmi ludda purisādako tvaṃNa taṃ na jānāmi vane vasantaṃAhaññaca puttosmi jayaddisassaMamajja khāda pituno pamokkhā  Jānāmi puttoti jayaddisassaTathāhi vo mukhavaṇṇo ubhinnaṃSudukkaraññeva kataṃ tavedaṃYo mattumicche  pituno pamokkho Na dukkaraṃ kiñcimahettha maññeYo mattumicche pituno pamokkhoMātucca  hetu paralokagamyā Sukhena saggena ca sampayutto Ahañca kho attano pāpakiriyaṃĀvi raho cāpi sare na jātuSaṅkhātajātimaraṇohasamasmiYatheva me idha tathā parattha Khādajja maṃdāni mahānubhāvaKarassu kiccāni imaṃ sarīraṃRukkhassa vate papatāmi aggāChādayamāno mayhaṃ tvamadesi maṃsaṃ Yo mata vicche  machasaṃ  Mātuva  vi machasaṃ  Paralokaṃ gantvā  machasaṃ   Idañca te ruccati rājaputtaCajāsi pāṇaṃ pituno pamokkhāTasmāniha tvaṃ  taramānarūpoSambhañaja kaṭṭhāni jalehi aggiṃ Tato have dhitimā rājaputtoDārū  samāhatva  mahantamaggiṃĀdipaṭitvā  paṭivedayitthaĀdipitodinā mahāyamaggi  Khādajja maṃ dāni pasayhakāriKiṃ maṃ muhuṃ pokkhasi haṭaṭhalomoTathā tathā tuyhamahaṃ karomiYathā yathā maṃ chādayamāno  adesi Ko tādisaṃ arahati khāditāyeDhamme ṭhitaṃ saccavādiṃ vadaññuṃMuddhāpi tassa vieleyya sattadhāYo tādisaṃ saccavādiṃ adeyya Idaṃ hi so brāhmaṇaṃ  maññamanoSaso avāsesi sake sarīreTeneva so candimā devaputtoSasatthuto kāmaduhajja yakkha  Cando yathā rāhumukhā pamutetāVirocate paṇṇareseva hānumāEvaṃ tuvaṃ porisādā pamutto viroca kampilla mahānubhāvaĀmodayaṃ pitaraṃ mātarañcaSabbo ca te nandatu ñātipakkho  Tato have dhitimā rājaputtoKatañajali pariyagā  porisādaṃ Anuññāto sotthi sukhī arogoPaccāgamā kampillamalinasatto Taṃ negamā jānapadā ca sabbeHatthārohā rathikā pattikā caNamassamānā pañajalikā upāgamuṃNamatthu te dukkarakārakositiJayaddisajātakaṃ Tasmāhi so tvaṃ  machasaṃ  Dāruṃ  machasaṃ syā Samāhitvā  machasaṃ  Sandipayitvā  vi machasaṃ Chādamāno  machasaṃ syā  idaṃhi so iti sabbattha indaṃ hi so iti bhavitabbaṃ Brāhmaṇa  machasaṃ  Pariggayaha  syā parisāya  machasaṃ Chaddantajātakaṃ  Kinnu socasi anuccaṅgi paṇḍusi varevaṇṇiniMilāyasi visālakkhi mālāva parimadditā Dohaḷo me mahārāja supinantenupaccagāNa so sulabharūpova yādiso mama dohaḷo Ye keci mānusā kāmā idha lokasmiṃ nandaneSabbe te pacurā mayhaṃ ahante dammi dohaḷaṃ  Luddā dve samāyantu ye keci vijite tavaEtesaṃ ahamakkhissaṃ yādiso mama dohaḷo Ime te luddakā devi katahatthā visāradāVanañña ca migaññu ca mamatthe catatajīvitā Luddaputtā nisāmetha yāvantettha samāgatāChabbisāṇaṃ gajaṃ setaṃ addasaṃ supine ahaṃTassa dantehi me attho alābhe natthi jīvitaṃ  Na no pitunaṃ na pitāmahānaṃDiṭṭho suto kuñajaro chabbisāṇoYamaddasā supine rājaputtiAkkhāhi no yādiso hatthināgo Disā catasso vidisā catassoUddhaṃ adho dasadisā imāyoKatamaṃ disaṃ tiṭṭhati nāgarājāYamaddasā supine chabbisāṇaṃ Ito ujuṃ uttariyaṃ  disāyaṃAtikkamma so satata giri buhanteSuvaṇṇapasso nāma giri uḷāroSupupphito kimpurisānuciṇṇo nāgarājāKathaṃ vijānemu gatiṃ gajasasa  Tattheva sā pokkharaṇi adureRammā sutitthā ca mahodikā caSampupaphitā bhamaragaṇānuciṇṇāEttha hi so nahāyati nāgarājā Sisaṃ  nahāto uppalamāladhāriSabbaseto puṇḍarikattacaṅgiĀmodamāno gacchati santike taṃPurakkhatvā mahesiṃ sabbabhaddaṃ  Tattheva so uggahetvāna vākyaṃĀdāya tuṇinañca dhanuñca luddoVituriya  so satta giri brahanteSuvaṇṇapasasaṃ nāma giriṃ uḷāraṃ Sītaṃ  machasaṃ  Catureyya  Āruyhaselaṃ bhavanaṃ kittarānaṃOlokayi pabbatapādamulaṃTatthaddasā meghasamānavaṇṇaṃNigrodharājaṃ aṭṭhasahassapādaṃ  Tatthaddasā kuñajaraṃ chabbisāṇaṃSabbasetaṃ duppasahaṃ parehiRakkhanti taṃ aṭṭhasahassanāgāĪsādantā vātajavappahārino Tatthaddasā pokkharaṇiṃ adureRammaṃ sutitthañca mahodikakañcaSampupphitaṃ bhamaragaṇānuciṇṇaṃYattha hi so nahāyati nāgarājā Disvāna nāgassa gatiṃ ṭhitiñcaVithissa yā nahānagatassa hotiOpātamāgañchi anariyarūpoPayojito cittavasānugāya  Khaṇitvāna  kāsuṃ phalakehi chādayiAttānamodhāya dhanuñca luddoPassāgataṃ puthusallena nāgaṃSamappayi  dukkaṭa  kammakāri Viddho ca nāgo koñcamanādi ghoraṃSabbeva nāgā ninnaduṃ ghorarūpaṃTiṇañca kaṭṭhañca cuṇṇaṃ karontāDhāviṃsu te aṭṭha disā samantato Vadhissametanti parāmasantoKāsāvamaddakkhi dhajaṃ isinaṃDukekhana puṭṭhassudapādi saññāArahaddhajo sabbhi avajjharūpo  Anikkasāvo kāsāvaṃ yo vatthaṃ paridabhessatiApeto damasaccena na so kāsāvamarahati Yo ca vantakasāvasasa silesu susamāhitoUpeto damasaccena sa ve kāsāvamarahati Katvāna  vi  Samappari  machasaṃ  Dukkata  vi   Samappito puthusallena nāgoAduṭṭhacitto luddakaṃ ajjhabhāsiKimatthāyaṃ kissa vā smama hetuMamaṃ vadhi kassa vāyaṃ payogo Kāsissa rañño mahesi bhadanteSā pujitā rājakule subaddāTaṃ  addasā sā ca mamaṃ asaṃsiDannehi atthohi ca maṃ avoca Bahu hi me dantayugā uḷārāYe me pitunañca pitāmahānaṃJānāti sā kodhanā rājaputtīVadhatthikā veramakāsi bālaṃ  Uṭṭhehi tvaṃ ludda kharaṃ gahetvāDanne ime chanda purā marāmiVajjasi taṃ kodhanaṃ rājaputtiṃNāgo hato handa imassa dantā  Uṭṭhāya so luddo kharaṃ gahetvāChetvāna dantāni gajuttamassaVaggu subhe appaṭime pathabyā Ādāya pakkāmi tato hi khipapaṃ Bhayadditā  nāgavadhena aṭṭāYe te nāgā aṭṭha disā vidhāvuṃAdisva  posaṃ gajapaccamittaṃPaccāgamuṃ yena so nāgarājā  Te tattha kanditvā roditva  nāgāSise sake paṃsukaṃ okiratvāAgamaṃsu  te sabbe sakaṃ niketaṃPurakkhatvā mahesaṃ sabbabhaddaṃ Ādāya dantāni gajuttamassaVaggu subhe appaṭime pathabyāSuvaṇṇarajihi samantamodareSo ludadako kāsipuraṃ upāgamiUpānesi so rājakaññāya danteNāgo hato handa imassa antā Sā taṃ adasa sāva  vi syā sā taṃ addasaṃ sā  machasaṃ Pathavyā  vi  Bhayaṭṭitā  machasaṃ syā Adisvāna  machasaṃ syā  Roditvāna  machasaṃ sāya Āgamiṃsu  machasaṃ syā   Disvāna dannāni gajuttamassaBhattuppiyassa purimāya jātiyāTattheva tassā hadayaṃ aphāliTeneva sā kālamakāsi bālā Mbodhipatto ca mahānubhāvoSitaṃ akāsi parisāya majhePucchiṃsu bhikkhu suvimuttacittāNākāraṇe pātukaronti buddhā Yamaddasātha dahariṃ kumāri kāsāvavatthaṃ anagāriyaṃ carantiṃSā kho tadā rājakaññā ahosiAhaṃ tadā nāgarājā ahosiṃ  Ādāya dantāni gajuttamassaVaggu subhe appaṭime pathabyāYo luddako kāsipuraṃ upāgamiSo kho tadā adavadatto ahosi Anāvasuraṃ cirarattasaṃsitaṃUccāvacaṃ caritamidaṃ purāṇaṃVitaddaro vitasoko visalloSayaṃ abhiññāya abhāsi buddho Ahaṃ vo tena kālena ahosiṃ tattha bhikkhavoNāgarājā tadā hosiṃ evaṃ dharetha jātakantiChaddantajātakaṃ Sambhavajātakaṃ  Rajjañca paṭipannasmā ādhipaccaṃ sucirata Mahattaṃ  pattu miccāmi vijetuṃ paṭhaviṃ imaṃ Dhammena no adhammena adhammo me na ruccatiKiccova dhammo carito rañño hoti pucirata Idha cevāninditā yena pecca  yena aninditāYasaṃ devamanussesu yena pappemu  brāhmaṇaSabbodhipatto ca mahānubhāvo iccādikā  imāgāthā dasabalassa guṇe vaṇṇenettahidhammasaṅgāhakattherehi ṭhapitā aṭaṭhakathā Suvirataṃ  machasaṃ  Mahantaṃ  vi machasaṃ  Pacca  machasaṃ Pappomu  machasaṃ syā  Yohaṃ atthañca dhammañca kattumicchāmi brāhmaṇaTaṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca brāhmaṇakkhāhi pucchito  Nāññatra vidhurā etadakkhātumarahati yaṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca kattumicchasikhattiya Ehi kho sahito gaccha vidhurassa upantikaṃNikkhaṃ rattasuvaṇṇassa haraṃ gaccha suvirataAbhihāraṃ imaṃ dajjā atthadhammānusiṭṭhiyā  Svādhipapāgā bhāradvājo vidhurassa upantikaṃTamaddasa mahābrāhmamā asamānaṃ sake ghare Raññohaṃ pahito duto koravyassa yasassinoAtthaṃ dhammañca pucchesi iccabravi yudhiṭṭhiloTaṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca vidhurakkhāhi pucchito  Maṅgaṃ me pidahissanti na taṃ sakkomi brāhmaṇaApidhetuṃ mahāsindhuṃ taṃ kathaṃ so bhavissatiNa te sakkomi akkhātuṃ atthaṃ dhammañca pucchito Bhadukāro ca me putto oraso mama atujoTaṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca gantvā pucchassu brāhmaṇa Svādhipapāgā bhāradvājo bhadukārassa sanatikaṃTamaddasa mahābrāhmamā nisinnaṃ sambhi vesmani  Raññohaṃ pahito duto koravyassa yasassinoAtthaṃ dhammañca pucchesi iccabravi yudhiṭṭhiloTaṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca bhadrakāra bravihi me  Maṃsakājaṃ  avahāya godhaṃ anupatāmahaṃNa te sakkomi akkhātu atthaṃ dhammañca pucchito Sañjayo nāma me bhātā kaṇiṭṭho me sucirataTaṃ tvaṃ atheñca dhammañca gantvā pucchassu brahmaṇa Svādippāgā bhāradvājo sañjayassa upantikaṃTamaddasa mahābrahma nisinnaṃ samahi vesamani Raññohaṃ pahito duto koravyassa yasasinoAtthaṃ dhammañca pucchise iccabravi yudhiṭṭhiloTaṃ tvaṃ atthāñca dhammañca sañajayakkhāhi pucchito  Sadā maṃ gilati  maccu sāyaṃ pato sucirataNa te sakekāmi akkhātuṃ atthaṃ dhammañca pucchito Sambhavo nāma me bhātā kaṇiṭṭho me sucirataTaṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca gantvā pucchassu buhmaṇa Abbhuto vata bho dhammo nāyaṃ asmākarucacatiTayo janā pitāputtā tesu paññāya no vidu Na naṃ sakkotha akkhātuṃ atthaṃ dhammañca pucchitāKathaṃ nu daharo jaññā atthaṃ dhammaññaca pucchito  Mā na ṃdaharoti uñāñāsi  apucchitvāna sambhavaṃPucchitvā sambavaṃ jaññā atthaṃ dhammañca brāhmaṇa Yathāpi cando vimalo gacchaṃ ākāsadhātuyāSabbe tārā  gaṇe loke āhāya atirocati Evampi daharupetā paññāyogena sambavoMā naṃ daharoti uññāsi apucchitvāna sambhavaṃPucchitvā sambhavaṃ jaññā atthaṃ dhammañca brāhmaṇa Yathāpi rammako māso gimbhānaṃ hoti brāhmaṇaAtevaññohi māsehi dumapupphehi sobhati Kāvaṃ  vi  Gilate  vi machasaṃ  Maññāsi  syā Tāra  vi syā sabbātara  machasaṃ  Evampi daharūpeto paññāyogena sambhavoMā naṃ daharoni uñāñāsi apucchitvāna sambavaṃPucchitvā sambhavaṃ chaññā atthaṃ dhammañca brāhmaṇa Yathāpi himavā brahme pabbato gandhamādanoNānārukkhehi sañachanno mahābhūtagaṇālayoOsadhehi ca dibebhi disā bhāti pavāti ca Evampi daharūpeto paññāyogena sambhavoMā naṃ daharoni uñāñāsi apucchitvāna sambavaṃPucchitvā sambhavaṃ chaññā atthaṃ dhammañca brāhmaṇa Yathāpi pāvako brahme acavimālī yasassimāJalamano vane gacche analo kaṇhavattatī Ghatāsano dhumaketu uttamāhevanaṃ dahoNisithe  pabbataggasmiṃ pahutedho  virocati Evampi daharūpeto paññāyogena sambhavoMā naṃ daharoni uñāñāsi apucchitvāna sambavaṃPucchitvā sambhavaṃ chaññā atthaṃ dhammañca brāhmaṇa Javena bhaduṃ jānanti balivaddañca  vāhiye Dohena dhenuṃ jānanti bhāsamānañca paṇḍitaṃ Evampi daharūpeto paññāyogena sambhavoMā naṃ daharoni uñāñāsi apucchitvāna sambavaṃPucchitvā sambhavaṃ chaññā atthaṃ dhammañca brāhmaṇa  Svādhippāgā bhāradvājo sambhavassa upantikaṃTamaddasa mahābuhmā kiḷamānaṃ bahīpure Nissite  syā nisidhe  machasaṃ  Bahutejo  syā machasaṃ Balibaḍañca  machasaṃ syā  Vāhane  machasaṃ      Raññohaṃ pahito duto koravyasasa yasassinoAtthaṃ dhammañca pucchesi iccabravi yudhiṭṭhiloTaṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca sambhavakkhāhi pucchito Taggha te ahamakkhissaṃ yathāpi kusalo tathāRājā ca kho taṃ jānāti yadi kāhati vā navā  Ajja suveti saṃseyya raññā puṭeṭhā sucīrataMā katvā avasi rājā attho jāte yudhiṭṭhilo Ajjhattaññeva saṃseyya raññā puṭṭho sucirataKummaggaṃ  na niveseyya yathā muḷho acetaso Attānaṃ nātivatteyya adhammaṃ na samācareAtitthe nappatāreyya  anatthe na yuto siyā Yo ca etāni ṭhānāni kattuṃ jānāti khattiyoSadā so vaḍḍhate rājā sukkapakkheva candimā Ñātinañca piyo hoti mittesu ca virocatiKāyassa bhedā sappañño saggaṃ so upapajjatitiSambhavajātakaṃ Māhākapijātakaṃ  Bārāṇassaṃ  ahu rājā kāsinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano Mittāmacca parikhuḷho  agamāsi migājiraṃ   Tattha brāhmaṇamaddakkhi setaṃ citraṃkilāsinaṃViddhasanaṃ koviḷāraṃva kisaṃ dhaonisanthataṃ Kumaggaṃ  machasaṃ  Nappakāreyya  nā  Bārāṇasyaṃ  syā bārāṇasiyaṃ  vi Vaḍano  machasaṃ  Paribyuḷho  syā machasaṃ  Migājinaṃ  syā machasaṃ migāciraṃ vi  Paramakāruññataṃ pantaṃ disvā kiccagataṃ naraṃAvaca byambhito rājā yakkhānaṃ katamonusi Hatthapādā ca te setā tato setataraṃ  siroGattaṃ kammāsavaṇṇante kilāsabahulovasi Vaṭṭanāvaḷisaṅkāsā piṭṭhi te ninantunnatāKāḷapabbāva te aṅgā nāññaṃ passāmi edisaṃ Ugghaṭṭapādo tasito kiso dhamanisatthatoChāto ātantarūposi kutosi  kattha gacchasi Duddasi appakārosi dubbaṇṇo bhimadassano Janetti yāpi te mātā na taṃ iccheyya passituṃ Kiṃ kammamakarā  pubbe kiṃ  avajjhaṃ aghātayiKibbisaṃ yaṃ karitvāna idaṃ dukkhaṃ upāgami Taggha te ahamakkhissaṃ yathāpi kusalo tathāSaccavādiṃ hi lokasmiṃ pasaṃsantidha paṇḍitā  Eko caraṃ gogavese muḷho accasariṃ vaneAraññe īriṇe  vivane nānākuñajarasevite Vāḷamigānucarite vippanaṭṭhosmi kānaneAcariṃ tattha sannāhaṃ khuppipāsāsamappito Tattha tindukamaddakkhiṃ  visamaṭṭhaṃ khubhukkhitoPapātambhi lambantaṃ sampannaphaladhārinaṃ Vātasitāni  bhakkhesiṃ tāni rucciṃsu me bhusaṃAtitto rukkhamāruyha  tattha hessāmi āsito  Ekamme bhakkhitaṃ āsi dutiyaṃ abhitatthitaṃTato sā bhañajatha  sākhā chinnā pharasunā viya Setataro  vi  Kutonu tvaṃ gacchasi  vi Bhimma  machasaṃ  Makaraṃ  vi  Kaṃ  vi Iriṇe  machasaṃ iraṇe  vi  Tiṇḍuka  machasaṃ syā Vātassitāni  machasaṃ syā  Rukkhamāruhi  vi machasaṃ Assito  syā  Bhajjitā  vi  Sohaṃ sahāva sākhāhi uddhapādo avaṃsiroAppatiṭṭhe anālambe giriduggasmiṃ pāpataṃ Yasmā ca vārigambhiraṃ tasmā na samapajjasiṃ Tattha sesiṃ nirānando anātho dasa rattiyo Athettha kapi magañchi gonaṅguṭṭho  darivaroSākhāhi sākhaṃ vicaranto khādamāno damapphalaṃ So maṃ disvā kisaṃ paṇḍuṃ kāruññamakarā  mayiAmbho konāma so ettha evaṃ dukkhena aṭṭitoManusso amanusso vā antānaṃ me pavedaya Tassañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā idaṃ vacanamabraviṃManussohaṃ byasampatto  sā me natthi ito gatiTaṃ vo vadāmi  bhaddaṃ vo tvañca me saraṇaṃ bhava Garusīlaṃ  gahetvāna vicaraṃ  pabbate kapiSilāya yoggaṃ katvāna nisabho etadabravi Ehi me piṭṭhimāruyha gīvaṃ gaṇhāhi bāhuhiAhaṃ taṃ uddharissāmi giduggata vegasā Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā vānarindassa sirimatoPiṭṭhimārūyha dhirassa gīvaṃ bāhāhi aggahiṃ So maṃ tato samuṭṭhāsi tejassī balavā kapiVihaññamāno kicchena giriduggata vegasā Uddharitvāna maṃ santo nisabho etadabraviIṅgha maṃ samma rakkhassu passupisasaṃ muhuttakaṃ  Sihā vyagghā ca dipi ca acchakokataracchayoTe maṃ pamatataṃ hiṃseyyuṃ te tvaṃ disvā nivāraya Evaṃ me parittātuna passupi so muhuttakaṃTadāhaṃ pāpakaṃ diṭṭhiṃ paṭilacchiṃ ayoniso Sampajjisaṃ  machasaṃ syā  Gonaṅguḷo  vi machasaṃ syā Kāruññamakaraṃ  vi machasaṃ syā  Vasampatto  vi machasaṃ syā Bhaddante  machasaṃ syā  Garuṃ  vi machasaṃ syā Vivari  vi machasaṃ  Bhakkho ayaṃ manussānaṃ yathā caññe vane migāYannunimaṃ vaditvāna chāto khādeyyaṃ vānaraṃ Asito ca gamisasāmi maṃsamādāya sambalaṃKantāraṃ nittharissāmi pātheyyaṃ me bhavissati Tato sīlaṃ gahetvāna matthakaṃ sannitāḷayiṃMama bhattakilantassa  pahāro dubbalo ahu So ca vegenudappatto kapi rudhiramakkhito Assupuṇṇehi nettehi rodanto maṃ udikkhati Māyyo maṃ kari bhaddante tvaṃ ca nāmedisaṃ kariTvaṃ ca kho nāma dighāyu aññe vāretumarahasi Aho vata re purisa tāva dukkarakārakaEdisā visamā duggā papātā uddhato mayā Anito paralokāva dubbheyyaṃ maṃ amaññathaTantena pāpadhammena pāpaṃ pāpena cintitaṃ Mā heva tvaṃ adhammaṭṭha vedanaṃ kaṭukaṃ phusiMāheva pāpakammantaṃ phalaṃ veḷuṃva taṃ vadhi Tayi me natthi vissāyo pāpadhammo asasaññato Ehi me piṭṭhito gaccha dissamānova santike Muttosi  hatthā vālānaṃ pattosi mānusiṃ padaṃEsamaggo adhammaṭṭha tena gaccha yathā sukhaṃ Idaṃ vatvā giricaro ruhiraṃ pakkhālya  matthakaṃAssuni sampamajjitvā tato pabbatamāruhi Sohaṃ tenābhisattosmi parilāhena addito Ḍayhamānena gattena vāriṃ pātuṃ upāgamiṃ Ganta  machasaṃ  Kapirubhira  vi machasaṃ pāpadhamme asasaññate  pu Muttoti  ni  Pakkhalya  vi machasaṃ syā  Aṭṭito bhavitabbaṃ  vi machasaṃ  Agginā viya santatto rahado edhiramakkhitoPubbalohitasaṅkāso sabbo me samapajjatha      Yāvanto udakhinduni kāyasmiṃ nipatiṃsu meTāvanto gaṇḍu jāyetha aḍḍhabeḷuvasādisā Pahinnā pagghariṃsu me kuṇapā pubbalohitāYena yeneva gacchāmi gāmesu nigamesu ca Daṇḍahatthā nivārenti itthiyo purisā ca maṃOkiṇṇā  putigandhena māssu orena āgamā Etādisaṃ idaṃ dukkhaṃ satta vassānidāni meAnubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ pubbe dukkaṭamattano Taṃ vo vadāmi bhaddaṃ vo yāvantettha samāgatāMāssu mittāna dubbhittho mittadubbho hi pāpāko Kuṭṭhi kilāsi bhavati yo mittānaṃ  idhaddubhiKāyassa bhedā mitattaddu  nirayaṃ so upapajjatītiMahākāpijātakaṃ  Dakarakkhasapañho Sace vo muyhamānānaṃ sattannaṃ udakaṇṇaveManussabalimesāno nāmaṃ ganheyya rakkhasoAnupubbaṃ kathaṃ datvā muñcesi dakarakkhino Mātaraṃ paṭhamaṃ dajjaṃ bhariyaṃ datvāna bhātaraṃTato sahāyaṃ datvāna pañcamaṃ dajjaṃ  brāhmaṇaṃChaṭṭhāṃ dajjamattānaṃ nevadajjaṃ mahosadhaṃ Posetā te janetti ca dīgharattānukampikāChambhi tayi paduṭṭhasmiṃ paṇḍitā atthadassiniAññaṃ upanisaṃ katvā vadhā taṃ parimocayi Okkiṇā  vi machasaṃ  Mittānidha dubbhati  machasaṃ  Mittadubbhi  machasaṃ Dajja  vi syā  Taṃ tādisaṃ pāṇadadiṃ orasaṃ gabbhadhāriṇiṃMātaraṃ kena dosena dajjāsi Daharā viya alaṅkāraṃ dhareti apiḷandhanaṃDocārike anikaṭṭhe ativelaṃ pajagghati Tatopi paṭirājānaṃ sayaṃ dutāni sāsatiMātaraṃ tena dosena dajjasi dakarakkhino Itthigumbassa pavarā accantapiyavādini Anuggatā  silavati chāyāva anapāyini Akkodhanā paññavati paṇḍitā atthadassiniUbbariṃ  kena desena dajjasi dakarakkhino Khiḍḍhāratisamāpannaṃ anatthavasamāgataṃSā maṃ sakānaṃ puttānaṃ ayācaṃ yācate dhanaṃ Sohaṃ dadāmi sāratto  bahuṃ uccavacaṃ dhanaṃSuduccajaṃ cajitvāna pacchā socāmi dummanoUbbariṃ kena desena dajjasi dakarakkhino Yenocitā jānapacā  ānitā ca paṭiggahaṃĀbhataṃ pararajjehi abhiṭṭhāya  bahuṃ  dhanaṃ Dhanuggahānaṃ pavaraṃ suraṃ tikhiṇamantinaṃBhārataṃ kena desena dajjasi dakarakkhino Mayovitā  jānapadā ānitā ca paṭigaghaṃĀbhataṃ pararajjehi abhiṭṭhāya bahuṃ dhanaṃ Dhanuggahānaṃ pavaro suro tīṇiṇamanti caMayāyaṃ sukhito rājā atimaññati dārako Upaṭṭhānampi me ayye na so eti yathā pureBhārataṃ tena desena dajjasi dakarakkhino Accantaṃ piya bhāṇini  machasaṃ syā  Anubbatā  syā anupubbatā  machasaṃ Uppariṃ  machasaṃ  Sārato  syā Janapadā  machasaṃ  Abhitthāya  machasaṃ Bahu  syā  Yenovitā  machasaṃ  Ekarattena ubhatyā tuvañca  dhanusekhavāUbho jātettha pañcālā sahāyā susamāvayā Cariyā taṃ anubandhittho  ekadukkhasukho tavaUssukko te divārattiṃ sabbakiccesu vyāvaṭo Sahāyaṃ tena dosena dajjāsi dakarakkhino Cariyāya  ayaṃ ayye pajagghittho mayā sahaAjjāpi tena vaṇṇena ativelaṃ pajagghati  Ubbariyāpi me ayye mantayāmi rahogatoAnāmantā pavisati pubbe appaṭivedito Laddhavāro katokāso ahirikaṃ anādaraṃSahāyaṃ tena dosena dajjāhaṃ dakarakkhino Kusalo sabbanimittānaṃ rudaññu  āgatāgamoUppāde supine yutto niyyāṇe ca āmuttamanikuṇḍalāNānājanapadā nāriyo devakaññupamā subhā Tvaññe  machasaṃ  Anubandho  machasaṃ  Vācaṭo  machasaṃ Cariyāma  machasaṃ  Sañajagghati  machasaṃ  Rutaññu  machasaṃ Paṭṭho  Vipulaggato  vi  Evaṃ sabbaṅgasampannaṃ sabbakāmasamiddhinaṃSukhitānaṃ piyaṃ dīghaṃ jīvitaṃ āyu khattiya Atha tvaṃ kena vaṇṇena kena vā pana hetunāPaṇḍitaṃ anurakkhanto pāṇaṃ cajasi duccajaṃ Yatopi āgato ayye mama hatthaṃ mahosadhoNābhijānāmi dhirassa aṇumattampi dukkataṃ Sace ca  kisamici  kāle maraṇaṃ me pure siyāPutte ca me paputte  ca sukhāpeyya mahosadho Anāgataṃ paccuppannaṃ sabbamatthaṃ vipassatiAnāparādhakammantaṃ na dajjaṃ dakrakkhino Idaṃ suṇotha pañcālā culaniyassa  bhāsitaṃPaṇḍitaṃ anurakkhatto pāṇaṃ cajati duccajaṃ Mātu bhariyāya  bhātucca sakhino brāhmaṇassa caAntano cāpi pañcālo channaṃ cajati jīvitaṃ Evaṃ mahatthikā  paññā nipuṇā sādhucintanī Diṭṭhadhamme hitatthāya samparāye sukhāya cātiDakarakkhasapañho Paṇḍarakajātakaṃ  Vikiṇṇavācaṃ aniguyhamantaṃ Asaññataṃ aparicakkhipāraṃ Bhayaṃ tamatveti sayaṃ abodhaṃNāgaṃ yathā saṇḍarakaṃ supaṇeṇā Yo guyhamantaṃ parirakkhaṇeyyaṃMohā naro saṃsati bhāsamānoTaṃ bhinnamantaṃ bhayamanveti khippaṃNāgaṃ yathā paṇḍarakaṃ supaṇeṇā Sacepi  machasaṃ  Mahiddhikā  vi machasaṃ syā Kismiñci  vi machasaṃ  Sādhucintini  machasaṃ Putte  machasaṃ  Atiguḷha  vi Culaneyasasa  machasaṃ  Aparirakki tāraṃ  vi Bhariyāca  vi  Nānumitto garuṃ atthaṃ gayhaṃ veditumarahati Sumitto ca asambuddhaṃ sambuddhaṃ vā anatthavā Vissāsamāpajjimahaṃ aceloSamaṇo ayaṃ sammato bhāvitattoTassāhamakkhiṃ vimaraṃ  guyhamatthaṃAtitamattho kapaṇaṃ rudāmi Tassāhaṃ purimaṃ brahme guyhaṃVācaṃ hi maṃ nāsakkhiṃ  saṃyametuṃTappakkhato hi bhayamāgataṃ meAtitamatthā kapaṇaṃ rudāmi  Yo ve naro suhadaṃ maññamānoGuyhamatthaṃ saṃsati dukkuline dosā bhayā athavā rāgarattoPallatthito  bālo asaṃsayaṃ so Tirokkhavāco asataṃ paviṭṭhoYo saṅgatisu mudireti vākyaṃĀsiviso dummukho tyāhu taṃ naraṃĀrā ārā saṃyame tādisambhā Antaṃ pānaṃ kāsi  kacandanañcaManāpitthiyo mālacchādanañcaOhāya gacchāmase sabbakāmeSupaṇṇa pāṇupagatāva tyambhā  Konidha  tiṇṇaṃ garahaṃ upetiAsmiñca loke pāṇabhu nāgarājaSamaṇo supaṇṇe athavā tavevaKiṃ kāraṇā paṇḍarakagaghito  Samaṇoti me sammatatto ahosiPiyo ca me vanasā bhāvitattoTassāhamakkhiṃ vivaraṃ guyhamatthaṃAtitamattho kapaṇaṃ rudāmi Na catthi satto amaro pathabyāPaññāvidhā natthi na ninditabbāSaccena dhammena dhiyā damenaAlabbhamabyāharati naro idha Vedetu  vi  Kāsākaṃ  vi Vivariṃ  vi machasaṃ syā  Mālamucchādanañca  machasaṃ Nāsakkhi  machasaṃ  Konavidhaṃ  machasaṃ Pallattho  vi pallatthiko  machasaṃ  Matā pitā paramā bandhavānaṃNāssa  tatiyo anukampakatthiTesampi guyhaṃ paramaṃ na saṃseMantassa bhedaṃ parisaṅkamāno Matāpitā bhaginibhātaro caSahāyā vā yassa honati sapakkhāTesampi guyhaṃ paramaṃ na saṃseMantassa bhedaṃ parisaṅkamāno Bhariyā ve purisaṃ vajjā komāri piyabhāṇiniPuttarūpayasupetā ñātisaṅghapurakkhatāTesampi guyhaṃ paramaṃ na saṃseMantassa bhedaṃ parisaṅkamāno  Na guyhamatthaṃ vivareyya rakkheyya naṃ yathā nidhiṃNa hi pātukato sādhu guyhamattho  pajānatā Thiyā guyhaṃ na saṃseyya amittassa ca paṇḍitoYo cāmisena saṃhiro bhadayattheno ca yo naro Guyhamatthamasambuddhaṃ sambodhayati yo naroMantabhedabhayā tassa dāsabhuto titikkhati Yāvanto purisassatthaṃ guyhaṃ jānanti mantitaṃTāvanto tassa ubbegā tasmā guyhaṃ na vissaje Vivicca bhāseyya divā rahassaṃRattiṃ giraṃ nātivelaṃ pamuñceUpassutikā hi suṇanti mantaṃTasmā manto khipapupeti bhedaṃ  Yathāpi assa nagaraṃ mahantaṃAdvārakaṃ āyasaṃ bhaddasālaṃSamantakhātāparikhāupetaṃEvampi me te idha guyhamantā Ye guyhamantā avikinṇavācāDaḷhā sadatthesu narā dujivhaĀrā amittā byavajanti tehiĀsivisāvāriva sattasaṅghā Tassa  machasaṃ  Guyho attho  vi  Hitvā gharaṃ pabbajito aceloNaggo muṇḍo vicarati ghāsahetuTamhi nu kho vivariṃ guyhavatthaṃAtthā ca dhammā ca apāgatambhā  Kathaṃ karo hoti supaṇṇarājaKiṃsilo kena vatena vattaṃSamaṇo caraṃ hitvā mamāyitāniKathaṃkaro saggamupeti ṭhānaṃ  Hiriyā titikkhāya damena khantiyāAkkodhano pesuniyaṃ pahāyaSamaṇo caraṃ hitvā mamāyitāni Evaṃkaro saggamupeti ṭhānaṃ Mātā ca puttaṃ taruṇaṃ tanujaṃ Sampassa taṃ sabbagattaṃ eretiEvampi me tvaṃ pāturahu dijindaMātāva puttaṃ anukampamāno  Bhandajja tvaṃ mucca  vadhā dujivhaTayo hi puttā nahi añño atthiAntevāsi dinnako aturajo ca rajassu puttaññataro me ahosi Icceva vākyaṃ visajji  supaṇṇoBhumyaṃ  patiṭṭhāya dijo dujivhaṃMuttajja tvaṃ sabbabhayātivattoThaludake hohi mayābhigutto Ataṅkinaṃ yathā kusalo bhisakkoPipāsitānaṃ rahadova sitoVesmaṃ yathā himasitaṭṭitānaṃ Evampi te saraṇambhaṃ bhavāmi  Sandhiṃ katvā amittena aṇḍajena jalākhujaVivariya dāṭhaṃ sayasi  kuto te bhayamāgataṃ Saṅketheva amittambhi mittasmimpi na vissaseAbhayā bhayamuppannaṃ api mulāni kantati Apaggambha  machasaṃ  Vissajji  machasaṃ Mamāyatāni  nā  Bhumyā  vi Tanujjaṃ  vi machasaṃ syā  Hima sisiraṭṭhitānaṃ machasaṃ  Muñca  vi machasaṃ  Kathannu vissase tyambhi yenāsi kalabho katoNiccayantena ṭhānabbaṃ so disabbhi na rajjati Vissāsaye na ca naṃ vissaseyyaAsaṅkito ca saṅkito bhaveyyaTathā tathā viññu parakkameyyaYathā yathā bhāvaṃ paro na jaññā  Te devavaṇṇā sukhumālarūpāUbho samā sujayo puññakkhandhāUpāgamuṃ kādambiyaṃ acelaṃMissibhūtā assavāhāva nāgā Tato have paṇḍarako acelaṃSayamevupāgamma idaṃ avocaMuttajjahaṃ sabbabhayātivattoNa hi nūna tuyhaṃ manaso piyambhā Piyo hi me āsi supaṇṇarājāAsaṃsayaṃ paṇḍarakena saccaṃSo rāgaratto ca akāsiṃ etaṃPāpaṃ kammaṃ sampajāno na mohā Na me piyaṃ appiyaṃ vāpi hotiSampassato lokamimaṃ parañcaSusasaññatānaṃ hi viyañjanneAsaññato lokamimaṃ carāsi  Ariyāvakāsosi anariyo cāsiAsaññato saññatasannikāsoKaṇhābhijātikosi anariyarūpoPāpaṃ bahuṃ duccaritaṃ acāri Aduṭṭhassa tuvaṃ dubbhi dubbhi ca pisuno casiEtena saccavajjena muddhā te phalatu sattadhā Tasmā hi mittānaṃ na dubbhitabbaṃVittadubbhā pāpiyo natthi aññoĀsittasatto nihato pathabyāIndassa vākyena hi saṃvaro hatotiPaṇḍarakajātakaṃ   Sambulājātakaṃ Kā vedhamānā girikandarāyaEkā tuvaṃ tiṭṭhasi saññaturuPuṭṭhāsi me pāṇipameyyamajjheAkkhāhi me nāmañca bandhave ca Obhāsayaṃ vanaṃ rammaṃ sihavyagghanisevitaṃAbhivādemi taṃ bhadde dānavāhaṃ namatthu te  Yo putto kāsirājassa sotthisenoti naṃ viduTassāhaṃ sambulā bhariyā evaṃ jānāhi danavaAbhivādemi bhaddante sambulāhaṃ namatthu te Vedehaputto bhaddante vane vasati āturoTamahaṃ rogasammattaṃ ekā ekaṃ upaṭṭhahiṃ Ahañca vanamuñachāya madhumaṃsaṃ migāvilaṃYadā harāmi taṃ bhakkho tassa nunajja nādhati Kiṃ vane rājaputtena āturena karissasiSambule pariciṇṇena ahaṃ bhattā bhavāmi te Sokaṭṭāya durattāya kiṃ rūpaṃ vijjate mamaAññaṃ pariyesa bhaddante abhirūpataraṃ mayā Ehimaṃ girimāruyha bhariyā mayhaṃ catussatāTāsaṃ tvaṃ pavarā hohi sabbakāmasamiddhati Nūna tarakavaṇṇābhe yaṅkikañci manasicchasiSabbantaṃ pacuraṃ vayhaṃ ramassujja mayā saha  No ce tuvaṃ maheseyyaṃ sambule kārayisassiAlaṃ tvaṃ pātarāsāya maññe bhakkhā bhavissasi  Tañca sattajaṭo luddo kaḷāro purisādakoVane nāthaṃ apassantiṃ sambulaṃ aggahi bhuje Adhipannā pisācena luddenāmisacakkhunāSā ca santuvasampattā patimevānusocati Na me idaṃ tathā dukkhaṃ yaṃ maṃ khādeyya rakkhasoYañca me ayyaputtassa mano hessati aññathā Na santi devā pavasanti nūnaNa hi nūna santi idha lokapālāSahasā karontānaṃ asaññatānaṃNa hi nūna santi paṭisedhitāro  Itthinamesā pavā yasassiniSantā samā agigirivuggatejāTañce tuvaṃ rakkhasādesi kaññaṃMuddhā ca hi santadhā te phaleyyaMā tvaṃ dahi muñca patibbatā sā Sā ca assamamāgañchi pamuttā purisādakāNiḷaṃ phalinasakuṇiva gatasiṅgaṃva ālayaṃ Sā tattha paridevesi rājaputti yasassiniSambulā utumattakkhā vane nāthaṃ apassati Samaṇe buhmaṇe vande sampannacaraṇe iseRājaputta apassanti tumbhambhi saraṇaṃ gatā Vande sihe ca byagghe ca ye ca yeca aññe vane migāRājaputtaṃ apassanti tumbha saraṇaṃ gatā Tiṇalatāni osadhyo pabbatāni vanāni caRājaputtaṃ apassanti tumbhamabhi saraṇaṃ gatā  Vande indivarisāmaṃ rattiṃ nakkhattamāliniṃRājaputtaṃ apassanti tumbhambhi saraṇaṃ gatā  Vande hāgirathiṃ gaṅgaṃ savantinaṃ paṭaṭiggahaṃRājaputtaṃ apassanti tumbhamhi saranaṃ gatā Vande ahaṃ pabbatarājaseṭṭhaṃ hivavantaṃ siluccayaṃRājaputtaṃ apassanti tumbhamhi saranaṃ gatā  Atisāyaṃ vatāgañaji rājaputti yassasiniKenanujja samāgañaji ko te piyataro mayā Idaṃ khohaṃ tadavocaṃ gahitā tena sattunāNa me idaṃ tathā dukkhaṃ yaṃ maṃ khādeyya rakkhasoYañca me ayyaputtasasa mano hesasti aññathā Corinaṃ bahubuddhinaṃ yāsu saccaṃ sudullahaṃThinaṃ bhāvo durājāno maccassevodake gataṃ  Tathā maṃ saccaṃ pāletu pālayisasti ce mamaṃYathāhaṃ nābhijānāmi aññaṃ piyataraṃ tayāEtena saccavajjena vyādhi te vupasammatu Ye kuñajarā sattasatā uḷārāRakkhanti rattindivaṃ uyyutāvudhāDhanuggahānañca satāni soḷasaKathaṃ vidhe passasi bhadde satatavo  Alaṅkatāyo padumuttarattavāVirāgitā passati bhaṃsagaggarāTāsaṃ sunitvā mitagitavāditaṃNa dāni me tāta tathā yathā pure  Suvaṇṇasaṅkaccadharā suciggahāAlaṅkatā mānusiyaccharūpamāSenopiyā tāta aninditaṅgiyo Khattiyakaññā paṭilobhayanti naṃ Sace ahaṃ tāta tathā yathā purePatiṃ tamuñachāya  punā vane bhareSammānaye maṃ na ca maṃ vimānayeItopi me tāta tato varaṃ siyā Yamantapāne vipulasmi ohiteNāri vimaṭṭhābharaṇā alaṅkatāSabbaṅgu  petā patino ca appiyāAkhajjha tassā maraṇaṃ tato varaṃ Api ce daḷiddā kapaṇā anāḷhiyā Kaṭādutiyā patinoca sā piyāSabbaṅgupetāyapi appiyāyaAyameva seyyā kapaṇāpi yā piyā  Sudullahitti purisassa yā hitāBhattitthiyā dullabho yo hitā caHitā ca te silavati ca bhariyāJaninda dhammaṃ cara sambulāya  Sace tuvaṃ vipule  laddhabhogeIssāvatinaṇā maraṇaṃ upesiAhañca te bhadde imā rājakaññāSabbeva te vacanakarā bhavāmātiSambulā jātakaṃ Gandhatindukajātakaṃ   Appamādo amatapadaṃ pamādo maccuno padaṃAppamattā na mīyanti ye pamattā yathā matā Aninditaggiyo  nā  Patita uñchaya  vi  Pañcaṅgu  machasaṃ Anāḷiyā  machasaṃ syā  Vippule  machasaṃ  gaṇḍatiṇḍuka  syā  Madā pamādo jāyetha pamādā jāyate khayoKhayā ca dosā  jāyanti mā mado bharatusabha  Bahu hi khattiyā jinā atthaṃ raṭṭhaṃ pamādinoAthopi gāmino gāmā anāgārā agārino  Khattiyassa pamattassa raṭṭhasmiṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaSabbe bhogā vinassanti rañño taṃ vuccate aghaṃ Nesa dhammo mahārāja ativelaṃ pamajjasiIddhaṃ phītaṃ janapadaṃ corā viddhaṃsayanti naṃ Na te puttā bhavissanti na hiraññaṃ na dhāniyaṃRaṭṭhe viluppamānambhi sabbabhogehi jiyasi Sabbabhogaparijiṇaṇaṃ rājānaṃ vāpi khatatiyaṃ Ñātimittā suhajjā ca na taṃ maññanti māniyaṃ  Hatthārohā  anikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakāTamevamupajivantā na taṃ maññanti māniyaṃ Asaṃvihitakammantaṃ bālaṃ dummanti mantinaṃSiri jahati dummedhaṃ jiṇṇaṃva urago tacaṃ Susaṃvihitakammantaṃ kāluṭṭhāyiṃ atanditaṃSabbe bogābhivaḍḍhanti gāvo sausabhāmiva Upassutiṃ mahārāja raṭṭhe jananapade caraTattha disvā ca sutvā ca tato taṃ paṭipajjasi  Evaṃ vedetu pañcālo saṅgāmo sarasamappito Yathāhamajja vedemi kaṇṭakena samappito Padosā  vi machasaṃ syā  Māpamādo bharamusaha  machasaṃ māpamādobhāratusabha  vi Khattiyā  vi  Khattiyā  vi  Hatthāruhā  vi Saramapipite  machasaṃ  Jiṇṇo dubbalacakkhusi na rūpaṃ sādhu passasiKiṃ tattha brahmadantassa yaṃ taṃ maggeyya kaṇṭeko Bavehattha  brāhmadattassa yohaṃ maggasmi brāhmaṇaArakkhitā jānapadā adammabalinā hatā Rattiñca corā khādanti divā khādanti tuṇḍiyāRaṭṭhasmiṃ kuṭarājassa bahu adhammiko jano Etādise bhaye tāta  bhayaṭṭā tāva  mānavāNillenakāni kubbanti vane āhatva  kaṇṭakaṃ  Kadāssu nāmayaṃ rājā brahmadatto marissatiYassa raṭṭhambhi  jiyanti  appatikā  kumārikā Dubbhāsitañhi te jammi anatthapadakovideKuhiṃ rājā kumārinaṃ bhattāraṃ pariyesati  Na me dubbāsitaṃ brahme kovidatthapadā ahaṃArakkhitā jānapadā adhammabalinā hatā Rattiñca corā khādanti divā khādanti tuṇḍiyāRaṭṭhasmiṃ kuṭarājassa bahu adhammiko janoDujjave dubbhatra  dāre kuto bhattā kumāriyo Evaṃ sayatu pañcālo saṅgāme sattiyā bhatoYathāyaṃ kapaṇo seti bhato phālena sāliyo Pahottha  vi  Maggosmi  vi  Jāte  machasaṃ Tāta  vi masaṃ  Āhanatvā  machasaṃ  Raṭṭhasmiṃ  vi machasaṃ Jivanti  vi  Appatinā  vi  Dubbare  machasaṃ  Adhammena tuvaṃ jamma buhmadattassa kujjhasiYo tvaṃ sapasi rājānaṃ aparajjhitvāna attano  Dhammena brahmadantassa ahaṃ kujjhāmi brahmaṇaArakkhītā jānapadā adhammabalinā hatā Attiñca corā khādanti divā khādanti tuṇḍiyāRaṭṭhasmiṃ kuṭarājassa bahu adhamamiko jano  Sā nūna puna re pakkā vikāle bhattamāhariBhattahāriṃ apekkhanto hato phālena sāliyo Evaṃ haññatu pañcālo saṅgāme asinā hato Yatāhamajja pahaṭo khirañcame pavaṭṭitaṃ  Yaṃ pasu khiraṃ chaḍḍheti pasupālañca hiṃsati Kiṃ tattha brahmadattassa yaṃ Gārayho brahme pañcālo brahmadattassa rājinoArakkhitā jānapadā adhammakhalinā hatā Attiñca corā khādanti divā khādanti tuṇḍiyāRaṭṭhasmiṃ kuṭarājassa bahu adhamamiko jano Caṇḍā aṭanakā gāvi yaṃ pure na duhāmaseTaṃ dāni ajja dohāma khirakāmehupaddutā  Evaṃ kaññatu pañcālo viputto vippasukkhatu yatāyaṃ kapaṇā gāvi viputtāparidhāvati Attanā  vi  Daḷha  vi  Pavattitaṃ  syā Phālaṃ vihiṃsatiṃ  machasaṃ  Garahato  vi  Yaṃ pasu pasupālassa pabbhameyya raveyya vāKonidha aparādhatthi burahmadantassa rājino Aparādho mahābrahme brahmadattassa jājinoArakkhitā jānapadā adhammakhalinā hatā Rattañca corā khādanti divā khādanti tuṇḍiyāRaṭṭhasmiṃ kūṭarājassa  bahu adhammiko janoKathaṃ no asikosatthā khirapā bhaññate pajā  Evaṃ khajjatu pañcālo hato yuddhe saputtakoYathābhamajja khajjami gāmakehi  araññajo Na sabbabhutesu vidhenti rakkhaṃRājāno maṇḍuka manussalokeNentāvatā rājā adhammacāriYā tādisaṃ jivamadeyyuṃ dhaṅkā Adhammarūpo vata Vessantaraṃ taṃ pucchāmi sakuṇā bhaddamatthu teRajjaṃ kāretukāmena kiṃsu kiccaṃ kataṃ varaṃ Cirassaṃ vata maṃ tāto kaṃso bārāṇasiggabhoPamatto appamattampi  pitā puttaṃ acodayi Paṭhameneva vitathaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaSabbe bhogā vinassanti rañño taṃ vuccate aghaṃ Siri ca tāta lakkhi  ca pucchitā etadabravuṃUṭṭhānaviriye pose ramāhaṃ anusuyake   Usūyake  dūhadaye purise kammadūsake Kālakaṇṇi mahārāja ramati cakkabhañjani So tvaṃ sabbesu  subhadayo sabbesaṃ rakkhito bhavaAlakkhiṃ nuda mahārāja lakkhyā bhava nivesanaṃ Salakkhi dhitisampanno puriso hi mahagagatoAmittānaṃ kāsipati mulaṃ aggañca chindati Sakkopi hi bhūtapati uṭṭhāne nappamajjatiSakalyāṇe dhitiṃ katvā uṭṭhāne kurute mano Gandhabbā pitāro devā sajivā  honti tādinoUṭṭhahato appamajjato anutiṭṭhanti Apamattaṃ  machasaṃ appamatta  syā  Ussuyyake  simu Vata  machasaṃ  Dussake  machasaṃ syā Tapo  vi machasaṃ  Sabbe subhadayo  machasaṃ Tākalakkhi  simu  Sājivā  machasaṃ syā Anusuyyake  sīmu  So appamatto akuddho tāta kiccāni kārayaVāyamassu ca kiccesu  nālaso vindate sukhaṃ Tattheva te vannapadā esāva anusāsaniAlaṃ mitte sukhāpetuṃ amittānaṃ dukhāya ca  Sakhi  tuvaṃ kuṇḍalini maññasi khattabandhuniRajjaṃ kāretu kāmena kiṃsu kiccaṃ kataṃ varaṃ Dveva tāta padakāni yattha sabbaṃ patiṭṭhitaṃAladdhassa ca yo lābho laddhassa anurakkhanā Amacce tātā jānāhi dhire atthassa kovadeAnakkhākitave  tāta asoṇḍe avināsake Yo ca taṃ tāta rakkheyya dhanaṃ yañceva te siyāSutova rathaṃ saṅgaṇhe so te kiccāni kāraye Susaṅgahitantajano sayaṃ vittaṃ avekkhiyaNidhiñca iṇadānañca na kare parapattiyā Sayaṃ āyaṃ vayaṃ caññā sayaṃ jaññā katākataṃNiggaṇhe niggahārahaṃ paggaṇhe paggahārahaṃ  Sayaṃ jātapadaṃ atthaṃ anusāsa rathesabhaMā te adhammikā yuttā dhanaṃ raṭṭhañca nāsayuṃ Mā ca megena kiccāni kāresi kārayesi vāVegasā hi kataṃ kammaṃ mando pacchānutappati Mā te adhisare mucca  sukhāḷhamadhikopitaṃKodhasā hi bahu phitā kulā akulataṃ gatā Mā tāta issarombhiti anatthāya patārayiItthinaṃ purisānanañca mā te āsi dukhudrayo Sakiccesu  machasaṃ syā  Sakkhisi  machasi Anakkhā kiṃ tave  machasaṃ  Muñca  machasaṃ  Apeta lomahaṃsassa rañño kāmānusārinoSabbe bhogā vinassanti rañño taṃ vuccate aghaṃ Tattheva te vannapadā esāva anusāsaniDakkhassudāni puññakaro asoṇḍo avināsakoSilavassu  mahārāja dussilo vinipātiko  Apucchimhā kosiyagottaṃ kuṇḍaliniṃ tatheva caTvaṃ dāni vadehi jambuka balānaṃ balamuttamaṃ Balaṃ pañcavidhaṃ loke purisasmiṃ mahaggateTattha bāhubalannāma carimaṃ vuccate balaṃ Bhogabalañca dīghāvu dutiyaṃ vuccate balaṃAmaccabalañca dīghuvu tatiyaṃ vuccate balaṃ Abhijaccabalañceva taṃ catutthaṃ asaṃsayaṃYāni etāni sabbāni adigaṇhāti paṇḍito  Taṃ balānaṃ balaseṭṭhaṃ aggaṃ paññābalaṃ varaṃPaññābalenupatthaddho atthaṃ vindati paṇḍito Api ce labhati mando phītaṃ dharaṇimuttamaṃ akāmassa pasayha vā añño taṃpaṭipajjati Abhijātopi ce hoti rajjaṃ laddhāna khattiyoDuppañño hi kāsipati sabbenapi na jīvati Paññā sutaṃ vinicchiniPaññā kintisilokavaḍḍhati Paññāsahito naro idhaApi dukkhepi sukhāni  vindati Paññañca kho asussusaṃ na koci adigacchatiBahusasutaṃ anāgamma dhammaṭṭhaṃ avinibbhujaṃ Pilavāssu  machasaṃ  Pasayhaṃ  sīmu  Kitti  machasi Sukhānu  machasaṃ  Yo ca dhammavibhāgañña kāluṭṭhāsi atandito Anuṭṭhahati kālena tamaphalaṃ  tassa ijjhati  Anāyatana  sīlassa anāyatana sevinoNa nibbindiyakārissa sammadattho vipaccati Ajjhantañca payuttassa tathāyatanasevinoAnibbindiyakārissa sammadattho vipaccati Yogappayogasaṅkhātaṃ sambatassānurakkhanaṃTāni tvaṃ tāta sevassu mā akamamāya randhayiAkammunā ca dummedho naḷāgāraṃva sidati  Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja mātāpitusu khantiyaIdha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja puttadāresu khantiyaIdha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja mittāmaccesu khantiyaIdha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja vāhanesu khalesu caIdha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja mittāmaccesu khantiyaIdha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja vāhanesu khalesu caIdha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja gāmesu nigamesu ca idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃgamissasi Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja raṭṭhesu janapadesu caIdha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja samaṇabrāhmaṇesu caIdha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi Matandito  machasaṃ  Tammaphalaṃ  sīmu  Sijjhati  machasaṃ Nānāyatana  vi  Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja migapakkhisu khattiyaIdha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja dhammo ciṇṇo  sukhāvahoIdha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja saindā  deva sabrahmakāSuciṇṇena divaṃ  pantā mā dhammaṃ rāja pamādo  Tattheva te vantapadā esāva anusāsaniSappaññasevikalyāṇi samattaṃ  sāmataṃ  vidutiTesakuṇajātakaṃ Sarabhaṅgajātakaṃ  Alaṅkatā kuṇḍalino suvatthāVeḷuriyamuttā tharukhaggabandhāRathesabhā tiṭṭhatha kenu tumbheKathaṃ vo jānanti manussaloke  Ahamaṭṭhako bhima  ratho panāyaṃKāliṅgarājā pana uggato ayaṃSusaññatānaṃ isinaṃ dasasnāyaIdhāgatā pucchitāyembha pañhe Vehāsayaṃ tiṭṭhati antalikkhePathaddhuno paṇṇaraseva candoPucchāmi taṃ yakkha mahānubhāvaKathaṃ taṃ jānanti manussaloke Yamāhu devesu sujampatitiMaghavāti taṃ āhu manussalokeSadevarājā idamajja pattoSusaññatānaṃ isinaṃ dassanāya Puviṇṇo  machasaṃ syā  Indā  machasaṃ syā Tidivaṃ  vi  Samatthaṃ  machasaṃ Samataṃ  machasaṃ  Bhimma  machasaṃ   Dūre sutā no isayo samāgatāMahiddhikā iddhiguṇupapantāVandāmi te ayire pasannacittoYe jivalokettha manussaseṭṭhā Gandho isinaṃ ciradikkhitānaṃKāyā cuto gacchati māḷutenaIto paṭikkamma sahassanettaGandho isinaṃ asici devarāja  Gandho isinaṃ ciradikkhitānaṃKāyā cuto gacchatu  māḷutenaVicitupupphaṃ surabhiṃva mālaṃGandheṃ etaṃ pāṭikaṅkhāma bhanteNa hottha devā paṭikkulasaññino Purindade bhūtapati yasassiDevānamindo maghavā sujampatiSa devarājā asuragaṇappamaddanoOkāsamākaṅkhati pañaha  pucchituṃ Konevimesaṃ idha paṇḍitānaṃPañhe puṭṭho nipuṇe vyākarissatiTiṇṇañca raññaṃ manujādhipānaṃDevānamindassa ca vāsavasasa  Ayaṃ isi sarabhaṅgo yasassiYato jāto virato methunasmāĀcariya  putto sucinitarūpoSo nesaṃ pañhāni vyākarisasti Koṇḍañña pañhāni viyākarohiYācanti taṃ isayo sādhurūpāKoṇḍañña eso manujesu dhammāYaṃ vuḍḍhamāgacchati esa bhāro Katāvakāsā pucchantu bhontoYaṃ kiñci pañhaṃ manasābhipatthitaṃAhaṃ hi taṃ taṃ vo viyākarissaṃÑatvā sayaṃ lokamimaṃ parañca  Tato ca maghavā sakko atthadassi purindadoApucchi paṭhamaṃ pañhaṃ yañcāsi abhipatthitaṃ Gacchati  mi  Pañhaṃ  machasaṃ pañeha  vi  Ācera  machasaṃ  Kiṃsu vadhitvā na kadāci socatiKissappahānaṃ isayo vaṇṇayantiKassidha vuttaṃ pharusaṃ khamethaAkkhāhi me koṇḍañña etamatthaṃ Kodhaṃ vadhitvā na kadāci socatiMakkhappahānaṃ iyo vaṇṇantiSabbesaṃ vuttaṃ pharusaṃ kamethaEtaṃ khantiṃ uttamamāhu santo Sakkā ubhinnaṃ vacanaṃ titikkhituṃSadisassa vā seṭṭhatarassa vāpiKathannu hinassa vaco khamethaAkkhāhi me koṇḍañña etamatthaṃ  Bhayā hi seṭṭhassa vaco khamethaSārambhahetu pana sādisassaYo cidha hinassa vaco khamethaEtaṃ khantiṃ uttamamāhu santo Kathaṃ vijaññā catumaṭṭharūpaṃSeṭṭhaṃ sarikkhaṃ athavāpi hinaṃCirūparūpeta caranti santoTasmā hi sabbesa vaco khametha  Na hetamatthaṃ mahatipi senāSarājikā yujjhamānā labhethaYaṃ khantimā sapapuriso labhethaKhantibalassupasamanti verā Subhāsitanena anumodiyānaAññaṃ taṃ pucchāmi tadiṅgha brūhiYathā ahu daṇḍaki nāḷikiro Athajjuno nalākhu cāpi rājāTesaṃ gatiṃ brūhi supāpakamminaṃKatthupapantā isinaṃ viheṭhakā Kisaṃ hi  vacchaṃ acakiriya  daṇḍakiUcchinnamulo sajano saraṭṭhoKukkulanāme nirayambhi paccatiTassa phuliṅgāni patanti kāye Nāḷikero  machasaṃ  Kisañhi  machasaṃ  Avakira  machasaṃ  Yo saññate pabbajite aheṭhayi Dhammaṃ bhaṇante samaṇe adusakeTaṃ nāḷikiraṃ sunakhā paratthāSaṅgamma khādanti viendamānaṃ  Athajjuno niraye sattisuleAvaṃsiro patito uddhapādoAṅgirasaṃ gotamaṃ heṭhayitvāKhantiṃ tapasasiṃ cirabrahmacāriṃ Yo khaṇḍaso pabbajitaṃ  achedasiKhantiṃ vadantaṃ samaṇaṃ adūsakaṃKālakhuviciṃ upapajja paccatiMahāpatāpaṃ kaṭaṭukaṃ bhayānataṃ Etāni sutvā nirayāni paṇḍitoAññāni pāpiṭṭhatarāni cetthaDhammaṃ care samanabrāhmaṇesuEvaṃ kā saggamupeti ṭhānaṃ  Subhāsitaṃ te anumodiyānaAññaṃ taṃ pucchāmi tadiṅgha brūhiKathaṃ vidhaṃ silavantaṃ vadantiKathaṃ vidhaṃ paññavantaṃ vadantiKathaṃ vidhaṃ sappurisaṃ vadantiKathaṃ vidhaṃ no siri no rahāti Kāyena vādāya ca yo dha saññatoManāsa ca kiñci na kāroti pāpaṃNa atatahetu alikaṃ baṇāti Tathā vidhaṃ silavantaṃ vadanti Gambhira pañhaṃ manasā vicintayaṃNāccāhitaṃ  kamma karoti luddaṃKālāgataṃ atthapadaṃ na riñcatiTathā vidhaṃ paññavantaṃ vadanti Achedayi  machasaṃ  Pabbajjitaṃ  machasaṃ  Baṇeti  machasaṃ Naccāhitaṃ  machasaṃ syā  Yo ce katañca katavedi dhīroKalyāṇamitto daḷhabhatti ca hotiDukhitassa sakkacca karoti kiccaṃTathāvidhaṃ sappurisaṃ vadanti Etehi sabbehi guṇehupetoSaddho mudu saṃvibhāgi vadaññaSaṅgāhakaṃ sakhilaṃ saṇhavācaṃTathāvidhaṃ no siri no jahāti  Subhāsitante anumodiyānaAññaṃ taṃ pucchāmi tadiṅgha brūhiSīlaṃ siriñcāpi satañca dhammaṃPaññacca kaṃ seṭṭhataṃ vadanti Paññā hi seṭṭhā kusalā vadantiNakkhantarājāriva tārakānaṃSīlaṃ siriñcāpi satañca dhammoAnvāyikā paññavato bhavanti Subhāsitante anumodiyānaAññaṃ taṃ pucchāmi tadiṅgha brūhiKathaṃkaro kintikārā kimācaraṃKiṃ sevamāno labhatidha paññaṃPaññāyidāni  paṭipadaṃ vadehiKathaṃ karo paññavā hoti macco Sevetha vuḍḍhe nipuṇe bahussuteUggāhako paripucchako  siyāSuṇeyya sakkacca  subhāsitāniEvaṃkaro paññavā hoti macco Sa paññavā kāmaguṇe avekkhatiAniccato dukkhato rogato caEvaṃ vipassi pajahāti chandaṃDukkhesu kāmesu mahabbhayesu Sacitarāgo pavineyya dosaṃMetataṃ cittaṃ bhāvaye appamāṇaṃSabbesu bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃAnindito brahmamupeti ṭhānaṃ Paññāyadani  vi machasaṃ  Capparipucchiko  simu  Sakkaccaṃ  machasaṃ   Mahiddhiyaṃ  āgamanaṃ ahosiTavamaṭṭhaka himarathassa cāpiKāliṅgarājassa ca uggatassaSabbesa  vo kāmarāgo pahino  Evaṃ metaṃ paravitatavediSabbesa no kāmarāgo pahinoKārāhi okāsamanuggahāyaYathāgatiṃ te abhisambhavema Karomi okāsamanuggahāyaTathā hi vo kāmarāgo pahinoPharātha kāyaṃ vipulāya pitāyāYathā gatiṃ me abhāsmabhavetha Sabbaṃ karissāma tavānusāsanaṃYaṃ yaṃ tuvaṃ vakkhasi bhuripaññaPharātha kāyaṃ vipulāya pitāyāYathā gatiṃ me abhāsmabhavema Katāyaṃ vacchassa kisassa pujāGacchantu bhonto isayo sādhurūpāJhāne ratā hotha sadā samāhitāEsā rati pabbajitassa seṭṭhā  Sutvāna gāthā paramatthasañahitāSubhāsitā isinā paṇḍitenaTe vedajātā anumodamānāPakkāmu devā devapuraṃ yasassino Gāthā imā atthavati subyañajanāSubhāsitā isinā paṇḍitenaYo kocimā aṭṭhakatvā suṇeyyaLabhetha pubbāpariyaṃ visseṃLaddhāna pubbāpariyaṃ visesaṃAdassanaṃ maccurājassa gacche Sālissaro sāriputto meṇḍissaro nāma kasasapoPabbato anuruddho ca kaccāyano ca devalo Anusisso ca ānando kisavaccho ca kolitoNārado puṇeṇā mantāniputto sesaparisā buddhaparisāSarabhaṅgo lokanātho evaṃ dharetha jātakantiSarabhaṅgajātakaṃ Mahatthiyaṃ  machasaṃ  Sabbesaṃ  vi Machasaṃ  Alamakhusājātakaṃ  Athabravi brahā indo vatrabhu jayataṃ pitāDevakaññaṃ parāhetvā sudhammāyaṃ alambusaṃ Misse devā taṃ yācanti tāvatiṃsā saindakāIsipalohike gaccha isisiṅgaṃ alambuse Purāyaṃ ambhe acceti vatavā brahmacariyavāNibbānahirato vuddho tassa maggāni avara Devarāja kimeva tvaṃ mameva tuvaṃ sikkhasiIsi palohike gaccha santi aññāpi accharā Mādisiyo pavarā ceva asoke vandane vaneTāsampi hotu pariyāyo tāpi yantu palobhikā  Addhā hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi santi aññāpi accharāTādisiyo pavarā ceva asoke nandāna vane Na tā evaṃ pajānanti pāricariyaṃ pumaṃgatāYādisaṃ tvaṃ pajānāsi nāri sabbaṅga sobhane Tvameva gaccha kalyāṇi itthinaṃ pavarā casiTaveva vaṇṇarūpena vasamānāpayissasi  Na cāhaṃ na gamissāmi devarājena pesitāVibhemi cetaṃ āsāduṃ uggatejo hi brāhmaṇo Aneke nirayaṃ pattā isimāsādiyā janāĀpantā mohasaṃsāraṃ tasmā lomāni haṃsaye Idaṃ vatvāna pakkāmi accharā kāmavaṇṇiniMissā missetu  micchanti isisiṅgaṃ alambusā Pavasamānayissasi  machasaṃ  Missitu  machasaṃ   Sā ca taṃ vanamogayha isisiṅgena rakkhitaṃBimbi  jālakasañachannaṃ samantā aḍḍhayojanaṃ Pātova pātarāsambhi udanahasamayaṃ paṭiAggiṭṭhaṃ parimajjantaṃ isisiṅgaṃ upāgami Kānu vijjurivāhāsi osadhi viya tārakāVicintavatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā Ādiccavaṇṇasaṅkāsā hemacandanagandhiniSaññaturu mahāmāyā kumarī cārudassanā Vilākā  mudukā suddhā pādā te suppatiṭṭhitāKamanā  kamaniyā te harantiyeva me mano Anubbā ca te ūru nāganāsasamupamāVimaṭṭhā tuyhaṃ sussoṇi akkhassa phalakaṃ yathā Uppalasseva kiñajakkhā nāhi te sādhu saṇṭhitāPurākañahañajanasseva durato paṭidisasti Duvidhā jātā urajā avaṇṭā sādhupaccudāPayodharā appatitā aḍḍhalākhusamā thanā Dighā kambutalābhāsā gīvā eṇeyyakā yathāPaṇḍarāvaraṇā vaggu catutthamanasannihā  Uddhaggā ca adhaggā ca dumaggaparimajjitāDuvijā nelasambhutā dinnā tava sudassanā Apaṇḍarā lohitantā jiñajukaphalasannibhāĀyatā ca visālā ca nto tava sudassanā Nātidīghā susammaṭṭhā kanakabyāsamocitāUttamaṅgaruhā tuyhaṃ kesā candanagandhikā Yāvatā kasigorakkhā vāṇijānañca yā gatiIsinañca parakkhantaṃ saññatānaṃ tapassinaṃ Bimba  machasaṃ  Vilaggā  machasaṃ  Gamanā  machasaṃ syā  Na te samasamaṃ passe asmiṃ paṭhavimaṇḍaleKo vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ  Na pañahakālo bhaddante kassapevaṃ gate satiEhi samma ramisasāma ubho asmāka assameEhi taṃ upaguhissaṃ ratinaṃ kusalo bhava Idaṃ vatvāna pakkāmi accharā kāmavaṇṇiniMissā missetumicchanti isiṅgaṃ alambusā  So ca vegena nikkhamma chetvā dandhaparakkamaṃTamuttamāsu veṇisu ajjhappatto parāmasī Tamudāvatta kalyāṇi paḷissaji susohanāCavi tamhi brahmacariyā yathā taṃ atha tositā Manasā agamā indaṃ vasantaṃ nandane vaneTassā saṅkappamaññāya maghavā devakuñajaro Pallaṅkaṃ pahiṇi khippaṃ sovaṇṇaṃ sopavāhanaṃSa uttaracchadapaññāsaṃ sahassapaṭikatthataṃ Tamenaṃ tattha dhāresi ure katvāna sobhanāYathā ekamuhuttaṃva tīṇi vassāni dhārayi Vimado tīhi vassehi pabujjhitvāna brāhmaṇoAddasāyi haritarukkhe samantā aggiyāyanaṃ Navapattavanaṃ phullaṃ kokilāgaṇaghositaṃSamantā sa viloketvā  rudaṃ assuni vattayi Na juhe na jape mante aggihuttaṃ pahāpitaṃKonu me pāricariyāya pubbe cittaṃ palobhayi Araññe me viharato yo me tejāha sambhataṃNānāratanaparipuṇṇaṃ nāvaṃva gaṇhi aṇṇave Paṭiloketvā  vi machasaṃ   Ahante pāricariyāya devarājena pesitāAvadhiṃ cittaṃ citetana pamādā tvaṃ na bujjhasi Imāni kira maṃ tako kasasapo anusāsatiKamalāsarisitthiyo tāyo bujjhesi māṇava Ure gaṇḍāyo bujjhesi tāyo bujjhesi māṇavaIccānusāsi maṃ tāto yathā maṃ anukampako  Tassāhaṃ vacanaṃ nākaṃ pitu vuddhassa sāsanaṃAraññe nimmanussambhi svājja jhāyāmi ekako Sohaṃ tathā karissāmi dhiratthu jivitena mePuna vā tādiso hessaṃ maraṇaṃ vā me bhavissati Tassa tejañca viriyañca ṭhitiṃ ñatvā suvaḍḍhitaṃSirasā aggahi pāde isisiṅgaṃ alambusā Mā me kajjha mahāvīra mā me kujjha mahāisiMahā attho mayā ciṇṇo tidasānaṃ yasassinaṃTayā pakampitaṃ  āsi sabbaṃ devapuraṃ tadā Tāvatiṃsā ca ye devā tidasānañca vāsavoTvañca bhadde sukhī hohi gaccha kaññe yathāsukhaṃ  Tassa pāde gahetvāna katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃAñjaliṃ paggahetvāna tambhā ṭhānā apakkami Yo tassā āsi pallaṅko sovaṇṇo sopavāhanoSauttaracchadapaññāso sahassapaṭikatthatoTameva pallaṅka māruyha agā devānasantike Tamokkamiva āyantiṃ jalantiṃ vijjutaṃ yathāPatito sumano citto devindo addā varaṃ Varaṃ ce me ado sakka sabbabhūtānamissaraNa isipalohikā gacche etaṃ sakka varaṃ varetiAlambusājātakaṃ Saṅkampitaṃ  Saṅkhapālajātakaṃ  Ariyāvakāsopi pasannanettoMaññe bhavaṃ mamaṃ pulaphalesanaṃ gatoIdāni āgacchati sāyakāle Ubhova gacchāmase asasamaṃ taṃYāva pitā mulaphalate etu  Aññe bahu isayo sādhurūpāRājisayo anumagge vasantiTeyeva pucchesi mamassamaṃ taṃTe taṃ nayissanti mamaṃ sakāse Na te kaṭṭhāni bhintāni na te udakamābhataṃAggipi te na bhāsito  kinnu mandova jhāyasi Hinnāni kaṭṭhāni huto ca aggiTapanipi  te samitā brahmacāriPiṭhañca mayhaṃ udakañca hotiRamasi tvaṃ brahmabhūto puratthā Abhintakaṭṭhosi anābhatodakoAbhāsitaggisi asiddhabhojanoNa me tuvaṃ ālapasi mamajjaNaṭṭhannu kiṃ cetasikañca dukkhaṃ Mayhaṃ  vi machasaṃ  Bahutā  machasaṃ  Ahesuṃ saṃyamanaṃ jaṭānaṃ Aññā ca tassa saññamani catassoNīlā pitā lohitikā ca setāTā saṃsare carato māṇavassaCirīṭisaṅghāriva pāvusambhi   Na mekhalaṃ  muñajamayaṃ dharetiNa santace  no pana babbajassa Tā jotare jaghanantare  visanatāSateritā vijjurivantalikkhe Akhilakāni ca avaṇṭakāniHeṭṭhā nābhyā  kaṭisamohitāniAghaṭṭitā niccakiliṃ karontiHaṃ tāta kiṃ rukkhaphalāni tāti Jaṭā ca tassa bhusadassaneyyāParosataṃ vellitaggā sugandhāDvedhāsiro sādhuvibhattarūpoAho nukho mayha tathā jaṭāssu Yadā ca so pakirati tā jaṭāyoVaṇṇena gandhena upetarūpāNiluppalaṃ vātasameritaṃva tatheva saṃvāti Jaṅghanantare  machasaṃ  Nabhyā  machasaṃ  Paṅko ca tassa bhusadassaneyyoNetādiso yādiso mayhakāyoSo vāyati erito māḷutenaVanaṃ yathā aggagimbhe suphullaṃ Nihanti so rukkhaphalaṃ paṭhabyāSucittarūpaṃ ruciraṃ dassaneyyaṃKhittañca tassa punareti hatthaṃHaṃ tāta kiṃ rukkhaphalaṃ nu kho taṃ Dantā ca tassa bhusadassaneyyāSuddhā samā saṅkhavarūpapantāMano pasādenti vivariyamānāNaha nūna so sākamakhādi Tadāhi  machasaṃ  Yadāddaṃ taṃ tiṭṭhantiṃ sabbagattaṃ manoramaṃTato sakassa cittassa nāvabodhāmi kañcinaṃ Ummādantimahaṃ diṭṭho āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalaṃNa supāmi divārattiṃ sahassaṃva parājito  Sakko ca me ummadantyā niviṭṭhoDadāmi te taṃ paricārayassu Puññā vidhaṃse  amaro na camahiJano ca me pāpamidanti jaññāBhuso ca tyassa manaso vighātoDatvā piyaṃ ummadantiṃ adiṭṭhā Janinda nāññatu tayā mayā narā paṭhabyā Añño nu te koci naro paṭhabyāSaddaheyya  lokasmiṃ na me piyātiBhuso ca tyassa manaso vighātoDatvā piyaṃ ummadantiṃ adiṭṭhā Addhā piyā mayha janinda esāNa sā mama appiyā bhūmipālaGaccheva tvaṃ ummadantiṃ bhadanteSīhova selassa guhaṃ upehi Idametadabravi  vi machasaṃ syā  Puñña vadhaṃse  machasaṃ puññā ca dhaṃse  syā Saddheyya  vi machasaṃ  Na piḷitā attadukkhena dhīrāSukhapphalaṃ kammaṃ paricchajantiSammohitāvāpi sukhena mattāNa pāpakammañca samācaranti Tuvañhi mātā ca pitā ca mayhaṃBhattā pati posako devatā caDāso ahaṃ tuyha saputtadāroYathā sukhaṃ sibba karohi kāmaṃ Yo issarombhīti kāroti pāpaṃKatvā ca so nuttapate  paresaṃNa tena so jīvati dīghamāyuṃDevāpi pāpena samekkhare naṃ Aññatakaṃ sāmikehi padintaṃDhamme ṭhitā ye paṭicchanti dānaṃPaṭicchakā dāyakā cāpi Añño nu te koci nāro paṭhabyāSaddaheyya lokasmiṃ na me piyātiBhuso ca tyassa manaso vighātoDatvā piyaṃ ummadantiṃ adiṭṭhā Nuttasate  machasaṃ  Saddheyya  vi machasaṃ  Diṭṭhā  machasaṃ Mamaṃ  vi vidhitumusasahe Sace tuvaṃ mayha satiṃ janindaNa kāmayāsi raviraseṭṭhaCajāmi naṃ sabbajanassa sibbaMayā pamutataṃ tato avhayesi naṃ Adusiyaṃ ce abhipāraka tvaṃCajāsi katte ahitāya tyassa vahā  ca te upavādopi assaNa cāpi tyassa nagarambhī pakkho Ahaṃ sabhissaṃ upavādametaṃNindaṃ pasaṃsaṃ garahañca sabbaṃMametamāgacchatu bhūmipālaYathā sukhaṃ sibba  karohi kāmaṃ  Yo neva nindaṃ na punappasaṃsaṃ Ādiyati garahaṃ nopi pujaṃSiri ca lakkhī ca apeti tamhāĀpo suvuṭṭhiva yathā thalambhā Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ ca sukhañca ettoDhammātisārañca manovighātaṃUrasā ahaṃ paṭicchissāmi sabbaṃPaṭhavi yathā thāvarānaṃ tasānaṃ Dhammātisārañca manovighātaṃDukkhaṃ ca nicchāmi ahaṃ paresaṃEkopimaṃ tārayissāmi ahaṃ bhāraṃDhamme ṭhito kaññaci ahāpayanto Sabbā  vi  Sivi  machasaṃ  Na panappasaṃsaṃ  machasaṃ  Saggūpagaṃ puññakamamaṃ janindaMā me tuvaṃ antarāyaṃ akāsiDadāmi te ummadantiṃ pasattoRājāva yaññaṃ  dhanaṃ brāhmaṇānaṃ Addhā tuvaṃ katena hitosi mayhaṃSakhā mama ummadanti tuvañcaNindeyyu devā pitaro ummadanti tuvañcaSatañca dhammāni sukittitāniSamuddavelāva duraccayāni  Āhuneyyo mesi hitānukampiDhātā vidhātā casi kāmapāloTayi hutā deva mahapphalā hiKāmena me ummadantiṃ paṭiccha Addhā hi sabbaṃ abhipāraka tvaṃ dhammaṃ acāri mama katatupattaAñño nu te ko idha sotthikattāDipado naro aruṇe jivaloke Tuvaṃ nu seṭṭho tvamanuttarosiTvaṃ dhammagutto dhammavidu sumedhoSo dhammagutto cirameva jivaDhammañca me desaya dhammapāla Tadiṅgha abhipāraka suṇohi vacanaṃ mamaDhammante desayissāmi sataṃ āsevitaṃ ahaṃ Yaññe  ma Cha Saṃ  Sādhu dhammaruci rājā sādhu paññāṇavā naroSādhu mittānamaddubbho pāpassākaraṇaṃ sukhaṃ Akkodhanassa vijite ṭhitadhammassa rājinoSukhaṃ manussā āsetha sitacchāyāya saṅghare Na cāhametaṃ abhirocayāmiKammaṃ asamekkha kataṃ asādhuYevāpi ñatvāna sayaṃ karontiUpamā imā myaha tuvaṃ suṇohi Gavañce taramānānaṃ jimbhaṃ gacchati puṅgavoSabbā tā jimbhaṃ gacchanti neteta jimbhaṃ gate sati Evameva manussesu yo hoti seṭṭhasammatoSo ce adhammaṃ carati pageva itarā pajāSabbaṃ raṭṭhaṃ dukhaṃ seti rājā ce hoti adhammiko Gavañce taramānānaṃ ujuṃ gacchati puṅgavoSabbā tā ujuṃ gacchanti neteta ujugate sati Evameva manussesu yo hoti seṭṭhasammatoSo cepi dhammaṃ carati pageva itarā pajāSabbaṃ raṭṭhaṃ sukhaṃ seti rājā ce hoti dhammiko  Na cāpahaṃ adhammena amarattamahipatthayeImaṃ vā paṭhaviṃ sabbaṃ vijetuṃ ahipāraka Yaṃ hi kiñci manussesu ratanaṃ idha vijjatiGāvo dāso hiraññañca vatthisaṃ haricandanaṃ Assitthiyo ca ratanaṃ maṇikañcaYañcāpi me candasuriyābhipālayantiNa tassa hetu visamaṃ careyyaMajjhe sivinaṃ usabhosmi jāto  Netā pitā uggato raṭṭhapāloDhammaṃ sivīnaṃ apacāyamānoSo dhammamevānuvicintayantoTasmā sake cittacase na vatte Addhā tuvaṃ mahārāja niccaṃ abyasanaṃ sivaṃKarissasi ciraṃ rajjaṃ paññā hi tava tādisi Etaṃ te anumodāmi yaṃ dhammaṃ nappamajjasiDhammaṃ pamajja khattiyo ṭhānā cavati issaro Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja mātāpitusu khattiyaIdha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja puttadāresu khattiyaIdha dhammaṃ sukhāvahoIdha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja saindā sabrahmakaSuciṇṇena divaṃ sattā mā dhammaṃ rāja pamādotiUmmādanti jātakaṃ Mahābodhijātakaṃ  Kinnu daṇḍaṃ kimajinaṃ ahuSabbalohitakodāni kālo pakkamituṃ mama  Abbhantaraṃ pure āsi tato majjhe tato bahiPurā niddhamanā hoti sayameva vajāmahaṃ Vitasaddhaṃ na seveyya udapānaṃva nodakaṃSacepi naṃ anukhaṇe bhajantaṃ na bhajati sevamānaṃ na sevatiSa ve manussapāpiṭṭho migo sākhassito yathā Accābhikkhaṇasaṃsagagā asamosaraṇena caEtena mittā jiranti akāle yācanāya ca Tasmā nābhikkhaṇaṃ gacche na ca gacche nabhājaye  vi machasaṃ  Nabhajati  machasaṃ nabhājati  vi Te  machasaṃ  Mayahaṃvā  vi mayahaṃ Tuyahaṃcāpi  vi machasaṃ  Passāma  vi   Udiraṇā ce saṅgatyā bhāvāya manuvattatiAkāmā akaraṇiyaṃ vā tameso muñcate iṇaṃPorāṇakaiṇamokkho kvidha pāpena lippati  So ce attho ca dhammo ca kalyāṇo na ca pāpakoBhoto ce vacanaṃ saccaṃ suhato vānaro mayā Attano ce hi vādassa aparādhaṃ vijāniyāNa maṃ tvaṃ garaheyyāsi bhoto vādo hi tādiso Akāmā karaṇiyamahi  machasaṃ syā  Limpati  machasaṃ syā Kuppeti  machasaṃ      Catunnaṃyevupādāya rūpaṃ sambhoti pāṇinaṃYato ca rūpaṃ sambhoti tattheva  anupagacchati suhato vānaro mayā Attano ce hi vādassa aparādhaṃ vijāniyāNa maṃ tvaṃ garaheyyāsi bhoto vādo hi tādiso  Āhu battavidhā loke bālā paṇḍitamāninoMātaraṃ pitaraṃ haññe atho jeṭṭhampi bhātaraṃHaneyya puttadāre ca attho ce tādiso siyā Yassa rukkhassa chāyāya nisideyya sayeyya vāNa tassa sākhaṃ bhañejayya mittadubbho hi pāpako Atha attho samuppanne samulamapi abbaheAttho me sambalenāsi suhato vānaro mayā So ce attho ca dhammo ca kalyāṇo na ca pāpakoBhoto ce vacanaṃ saccaṃ suhato vānaro mayā Attano ce hi vādassa aparādhaṃ vijāniyāNa maṃ tvaṃ garaheyyāsi bhoto vādo hi tādiso  Ahetuvādo puriso yo ca issarakuttikoPubbekati ca ucchedi yo ca khattavidho naro Tatthevānupa  vi machasaṃ  Ete asappurisā loke bālā paṇḍitamāninoKareyya tādiso pāpaṃ atho aññampi kārayeAsappurisasaṃsaggo dukkaṭo kaṭukudrayo Urabbharūpena khakāsu  pubbeAsaṅkito ajayuthaṃ upetiHanatvā uraṇiṃ ajiyaṃ  ajañcaCitrāsayitvā yena kāmaṃ paleti  Tathā vidheke samaṇabrāhmaṇāseChadanaṃ katvā vañcayanti manusseAnāsakā thaṇḍilaseyyakā caRajojallaṃ ukkuṭikappadhānaṃPariyāyabhantañca apāṇakattaṃ Pāpācārā arahanto vadānā Ete asappurisā loke bālā paṇḍitamāninoKareyya tādiso pāpaṃ atho aññampi kārayeAsappurisasaṃsaggo dukkaṭo kaṭukudrayo Yamāhu natthi viriyanti hetuñca apavadanti  yeParakāraṃ attakārañca ye tucchaṃ samavaṇṇayuṃ Ete asappurisā loke bālā paṇḍitamāninoKareyya tādiso pāpaṃ atho aññampi kārayeAsappurisasaṃsaggo dukkaṭo  kaṭukudrayo Sace hi viriyaṃ nāsasa kammaṃ kalyāṇapāpakaṃNa bhare vaḍḍhakiṃ  rājā napi yantāni  kāraye Yasmā ca viriyaṃ atthi kammaṃ kalyāṇapāpakaṃTasmā yantāni kāreti rājā bharati vaḍḍhakiṃ Yadi vassasataṃ devo na vasse na himaṃ pateUcchijjeyya ayaṃ loko vinasseyya ayaṃ pajā Vakasusa  machasaṃ vakāsu  vi  Ajikaṃ  machasaṃ  Apāṇakattā  machasaṃ syā Ahetuñca pavadantiye  machasaṃ Dukkhanto  machasaṃ  Vaḍḍhati  machasaṃ  Tantāni  machasaṃ  Yasmā ca vassati devo himaṃ cāpi phusiyatiTasmā sassāni paccanti raṭṭhañca pallate viraṃ Gamañce taramānānaṃ jimbhaṃ gacchati puṅgavoSabbā tā jimbhaṃ gacchanti nette jimbhaṃ gate sati Evameva manussesu yo hoti seṭṭhasammatoSo ce adhammaṃ carati pageva itarā pajāSabbaṃ raṭṭhaṃ dukkhaṃ seti rājā ce hoti adhammiko Gamañce taramānānaṃ ujuṃ gacchati puṅgavoSabbā tā ujuṃ gacchanti nette ujugate sati Evameva manussesu yo hoti seṭṭhasammatoSo ce dhammaṃ carati pageva itarā pajāSabbaṃ raṭṭhaṃ dukkhaṃ seti rājā ce hoti adhammiko Mahārukkhassa phalino āmaṃ chindati yo phalaṃRasañcassa na jānāti bijañcassa vinassati  Mahārukkhupamaṃ raṭṭhaṃ adhammena yo pasasāsatiRasañcassa na jānāti raṭṭhañcassa vinassati Mahārukkhassa phalino pakkaṃ chindati yo phalaṃRañcassa vijānāti bijañcassana nassati Mahārukkhupamaṃ raṭṭhaṃ dhammena yo pasāsatiRasañcassa vijāniti raṭṭhañcassa na nassati Yoca rājā janapadaṃ adhammena pasāsatiSabbosadhihi so rājā viruddhaṃ hoti khattiyo Bhimañcānuphusayati  machasaṃ himaṃcānu phuseyyati  vi  Ujuṃ  machasaṃ  Tatheva negame hiṃsaṃ ye yuttā kayavikkayeOjadānabalikāre sa kosena virujjhati Pabhāravarakhettaññu saṅgāme katanissameUssite hiṃsayaṃ rājā sabalena virujjhati Tatheva isayo hiṃsaṃ saṃyame brahmacārinoAdhammacāri khattiyo so saggena virujjhati Yo ca rājā adhammaṭṭho bhariyaṃ hatta adūsakaṃLuddaṃ pasavate pāpaṃ puttehi ca virujjhati Dhammañcare jānapade negamesu balesu caIsayo ca na hiṃseyyaṃ puttadāre samañcare Sa tādiso bhumipati raṭṭhapālo akodhanoSāmante sampakampeti indeva asurādhipoti vi machasaṃ   hānaṃ  machasaṃ syā Saṭṭhinipāto Soṇakajātakaṃ  Kassa sutvā sataṃ dammi sahassaṃ daṭṭhu soṇakaṃKo me soṇaka makkhāti sahāyaṃ paṃsukiḷitaṃ Atha bravi māṇavako daharo pañcacuḷakoMayhaṃ sutvā sataṃ dehi sahassaṃ daṭṭhu soṇakaṃAhaṃ soṇakamakkhissaṃ sahāyaṃ paṃsukiḷitaṃ  Katarasmiṃ so janapade raṭṭhesu nigamesu caKattha te soṇako diṭṭho taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito Taveva deva vijite tavecuyyānabhumiyāUjuvaṃsā mahāsālā nilobhāsā manoramāTiṭṭhanti meghasamānā rammā aññoññanissitā Tesaṃ mulasmiṃ soṇako jhāyati anupādanoUpādānesu lokesu dayhamānesu nibbuto Tato ca rājā pāyāsi senāya caturaṅgiyāKārāpetvā samaṃ maggaṃ agamā yena soṇako Uyyānabhumiṃ gantvāna vicaranto brahāmaneĀsinaṃ soṇakaṃ dakkhi dayhamānesu nibbutaṃ Kapaṇovatāyaṃ bhikkhu muṇḍo saṅghāṭipārutoAmātiko apitiko rukkhamulasmiṃ jhāyati Imaṃ vākyaṃ nisāmetvā soṇako etadabraviNa rājā kapaṇo hoti dhammaṃ kāyena phassayaṃ Diṭṭha  machasaṃ syā  Makkhāsi  machasaṃ  Saha paṃsukiḷitaṃ  vi Soṇakakkhissaṃ  machasaṃ  Katamasmiṃ  machasaṃ  Katthasoṇakamadadakkhi machasaṃ  Jivite  machasaṃ  Mulamhi  machasaṃ  Ḍayahamānesu  vi machasaṃ syā   Yodha dhammaṃ niraṃkatvā adhammamanuvattatiSa rāja kapaṇo hoti pāpo pāpaparāyano Arindamoti me nāmaṃ kāsirājāti maṃ viduKacci bhoto sukhaseyyā idha pattassa soṇaka Sadāpi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhunoNa tesaṃ koṭṭhe openti na kumbhiṃ na kaḷopiyaṃParaniṭṭhita mesānā tena yāpenati subbatā Dutiyampi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhunoAnavajjapiṇḍo bhottabbo na ca kocuparodhati Tatiyampi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhunoNibbutapiṇḍo bhottabbo na ca kocuparodhati Catutthampi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhunoMuttassa raṭṭhe carato saṅgho yassa na vijjati Pañcampi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhunoNagarambhi dayhamānamhi nāssa kiñci adayhatha  Chaṭṭhampi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhunoRaṭṭhe vilumpamānamhi nāssa kiñci ahāratha Sattamampi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhunoCorehi rakkhitaṃ maggaṃ ye caññe paripatthikā pattacivaramādāya sotthiṃ gacchati subbato Aṭṭhamampi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhunoYaṃ yaṃ disaṃ pakakamati anapekkhova gacchati Paritiṭṭhita  vi machasaṃ syā  Nibbuto  vi machasaṃ  Āharatha  machasaṃ   Bahuni samaṇabhaduni ye tvaṃ bhikkhu pasaṃsasiAhañca giddho kāmesu kathaṃ kāhāmi soṇaka Piyā me mānusā kāmā atho dibyāpi me piyāAtha kena nu vaṇṇena abho loke labhambhase  Kāmesu giddhā kāmaratā kāmesu adhimucchitāNarā pāpāni katvāna upapajjanti duggatiṃ Ye ca kāme pahatvāna nikkhantā akutobhayāEkodibhāvādhigatā na te gacchanti duggatiṃ Upamante karissāmi taṃ suṇohi arandamaUpamāyapidhekacce atthaṃ jānanti paṇḍitā Gaṅgāya kuṇapaṃ disvā cuyhamānaṃ mahaṇṇaveVāyaso samavintesi appapañño acetaso Yānañca vatidaṃ laddhaṃ bhakkhovāyaṃ anapapakoTattha rattiṃ tattha divā tattheva nirato mano Khādaṃ nāgassa maṃsāni picaṃ bhāgirathodakaṃSampassaṃ vanacetyāni na palettha vihaṅgamo Tañca otaraṇi gaṅgā pamatataṃ kuṇape rataṃSamuddaṃ ajjhagāhāsi agati yattha pakkhinaṃ So ca bhakkhaparikkhiṇo uppatitvā vihaṅgamoNa pacchato na purato nuttaraṃ nopi dakkhiṇaṃ Dīpaṃ so na ajjhagañchi agati yattha pakkhinaṃSo ca tattheva pāpattha yathā dubbalako tathā Bahu pi bhadrā etesaṃ  machasaṃ bahupi bhadrakā ete  vi  Dibbāpi  vi  Upamāyavidhekacce  machasaṃ  Napaḷetha  machasaṃ  Upadatvā  vi machasaṃ  Tañca sāmuddikā macchā kumahilā makarā susuPasayhakārā khādiṃsu endamānaṃ vipakkhinaṃ Evameva tuvaṃ rāja ye caññe kāmabhoginoGiddhā ce na vamissanti kākapaññāya te vidu Esā te upamā rāja atthasandassani katāTvaṃ ca paññāyase tena yadi kāhasi vā na vā  Ekavācampi dve vācaṃ bhaṇeyya anukampakoTatuttariṃ na rajjenamatthiko Ajjeva pabbajissāmi ko jaññā maraṇaṃ suveMāhaṃ kākova dummedho kāmānaṃ vasamanacagaṃ Atthi te daharo putto dighāvu raṭṭhavaḍḍhanoTaṃ rajje abhisiñcassu so no rājā bhavissati Khippaṃ kumāraṃ ānetha dighāvuṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃTaṃ rājje abhisiñcissaṃ so vo rājā bhavissati Tato kumāraṃ ānesuṃ dighāvuṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃTaṃ disvā ālapi rājā ekaputtaṃ manoramaṃ Saṭṭhi gāmasahassāni paripuṇṇāni sabbasoTe putta paṭipajjassu rajjaṃ niyyādayāmi te Vipakkhakaṃ  machasaṃ  Kākapaññāca  machasaṃ  Taduttari  machasaṃ  Ayiyassa vi  Sudadāveyyattamāgatā  machasaṃ suduveyyatati māgatā  vi tomaraṅkusapāṇihiTe putta paṭipajjassu rajjaṃ niyyādayāmi te Ajjeva pabbajissāmi ko jaññā maraṇaṃ suveMāhaṃ kākova dummedho kāmānaṃ vasamanavagaṃ Saṭṭhiassasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhusitāĀjāniyā ca Saṭṭhiassasahassāni sannaddhā ussitaddhajāDipā athopi veyyagghā sabbālaṅkārabhusitā Ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihiTe putta paṭipajjassu rajjaṃ niyyādayāmi te Ajjeva pabbajissāmi ko jaññā dummedho kāmānaṃ vasamanvagaṃ Soḷasitthisahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhusitāVicitravatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalāTā putta paṭipajjassu rajjaṃ niyyādayāmi te Veyagghaṃ  machasaṃ  Ajjeva pabbajissāmi ko jaññā maraṇaṃ suveMāhaṃ kākova dummedho kāmānaṃ vasamanavagaṃ Daharasseva me tāta mātā matāti me sutaṃTayā vinā ahaṃ tāta jīvitumpi na ussahe Yathā āraññakaṃ nāgaṃ poto anveti pacchatoJessantaṃ giriduggesu samesu visamesu ca Evaṃ taṃ anugacchāmi puttamādāya gacchatoSubharo te bhavissāmi na te hessāmi dubbharo Yathā sāmuddikaṃ nāvaṃ vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃVohāro tattha gaṇheyya vāṇijā byasani siyā Imaṃ kumāraṃ pāpetha pāsādaṃ rativaḍḍhanaṃ Tattha kambusahatthāyo yathā sakkaṃva accharāTā naṃ tattha ramessanti tāhi ceso ramissati Tato kumāraṃ pāpesuṃ pāsādaṃ rativaḍḍhanaṃTaṃ disvā avacuṃ kaññā dighāvuṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃ Devatānusi gandhabbo ādu sakko purindadoKo vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ Namhi devo na gandhabbo napi sakko purindadoKāsi rañño ahaṃ putto dighāvu raṭṭhavaḍḍhanoMamaṃ bharatha bhaddaṃ vo ahaṃ bhattā bhavāmi vo Taṃ tattha avacuṃ kaññā dighāvuṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃKuhiṃ rā anuppetto ito rājā kuhiṃ gato Desasantaṃ  machasaṃ  Byasanaṃ  machasaṃ  Evamevāyaṃputatakali  vi machasaṃ Avacaṃ  machasaṃ  Namhi  machasaṃ  Te  machasaṃ  Paṅkaṃ rājā atikkanto thale rājā patiṭṭhitoAkaṇṭakaṃ agahanaṃ paṭipanno mahāpathaṃ Ahañca paṭipannosmi maggaṃ duggatigāminaṃ sakaṇṭakaṃ sagahanaṃ yenagacchanti duggatiṃ Tassa te svāgataṃ rājā sihassova giribbajaṃAnusāsa mahārāja tvaṃ no sabbāsamissarotiSoṇakajātakaṃ Saṅkiccajātakaṃ   Disvā nisinnaṃ rājānaṃ Gacchāmi  vi Machasaṃ  Nikkhipa  machasaṃ  Thapayitvā  machasaṃ  Isiṃ pucchāmi saṅkiccaṃ isinaṃ sādhusammataṃĀsinaṃ dāyapassasmiṃ isisaṅghapurakkhataṃ  Kaṃ gatiṃ pepacca gacchanti narā dhammāticārinoAticiṇṇo mayā dhammo tamme akkhāhi pucchito Isi avaca saṅkicco kāsinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃĀsinaṃ dāyapassasmiṃ mahārāja suṇohi me Uppathena vajantassa yo maggamanusāsatiTassa ce vacanaṃ kayirā nāssa maggeyya kaṇṭako Adhammaṃ paṭipannassa yo dhammamanusāsatiTassa te vacanaṃ kayirā na so gaccheya duggatiṃ  Dhammo patho mahārāja adhammo pana uppathoAdhammo nirayaṃ neti dhammo pāpeti suggatiṃ Adhammacārino rāja narā visamajivinoYaṃ gatiṃ pecca gacchanti niraye te suṇohi me Sañachivo kāḷasutto ca saṅghāto dve ca roruvāAthāparo mahāvici tapano ca patāpano Iccete aṭṭha nirayā akkhātā janapadaṃ tāpane pecca  paccati Yo ca vassasahassānaṃ  sataṃ dibyāni  paccatiAcacisaṅghapareto so dukkhaṃ vedeti vedanaṃ  Tassa aggisikhā kāyā niccharanti pabhassarāTejobhakkhassa gattāni lomaggehi Sace hi vacanaṃ saccaṃ aññesaṃ yadi vā mamaNeva tuyhaṃ pati atthi añño sihassarā kusā  Nekkhaṃ  givante kāressa patvā khujje kusavātiṃSace maṃ nāganāsuru olokeyya pabhāvati Nekkhaṃ givante kāressaṃ Kārissaṃ  machasaṃ  Anāganāsuraṃ  machasaṃ syā nāganāsuraṃ  vi Umbhāpeyya  vi machasaṃ  Pambhāpeyya  vi machasaṃ  Pāṇinā  machasaṃ   Nahi nunāyaṃ rājaputti rājaputti kuse sātampi vindatiĀḷārike bhate padassāmi ye maṃ hattumidhāgatā Athuṭṭhuhī rājaputti sāmā koseyyavāsiniAssupuṇṇehi nettehi dāsigaṇapurakkhatā  Taṃ nūna kakkupasevitaṃ mukhaṃĀdāsadantā tharupaccavekkhitaṃSubhaṃ sunteṃ virajaṃ
