candanasāralittāChannā vane ujjhitā khantiyehiGayha dhaṅko gacchati yenakāmaṃ Khile  machasaṃ  Sivaṭhikāya  machasaṃ  Parikaḍḍhiyanti  machasaṃ  Te nūna tālupanibhe alambeNisevite kāsikacandanenaThanesu me lambisasti sigālo Mātāva putto taruṇo tanujo Taṃ nūna soṇiṃ puthulaṃ sukoṭṭhitaṃNisevitaṃ kañcana mekhalāhi Chinnaṃ vane khantiyehi avatthaṃSigālasaṅghā parikaḍḍhayanti  Soṇā dhaṅkā sigālā ca ye caññe santi dāṭhinoAjarā nūna hessanti bhakkhayitvā pabhāvatiṃ Sace maṃsāni bhāresuṃ  khantiyā duragāminoAṭṭhini amma yācitvā anupanthe  ahātha naṃ Khentāni amma kāretvā kaṇikārettha ropayaYadā te puppitā assu hemantānaṃ himaccayeSareyyātha mamaṃ amma evaṃvaṇṇā pabhāvati  Tassā mātā udaṭṭhāsi khattiyā devavaṇṇinīDisvā asiñca suṇañca rañño maddassa thipure  Iminā nūna asinā susaññaṃ tanumajjhimaṃDhitaraṃ mama hanatvāna  khantiyānaṃ padassasi Na me akāsi vacanaṃ atthakāmāya puttikeSājja lohitasaññachantā gañachisi  yamasādhanaṃ Evamāpajjati poso pāpiyaññaca nigacchatiYo ve hitānaṃ vacanaṃ na karaṃ atthadassinaṃ Sace tvaṃ amma dhāresi  kumāraṃ cārudassanaṃKusena jātaṃ khattiyaṃ suvaṇṇamaṇimekhalaṃPujitaṃ ñātisaghehi na gañchisi yamakkhayaṃ Yatthassu bherī nadati kuñajaro paṭikujjati Khattiyānaṃ kule bhadde kinnu sukhataraṃ tato Diṅgālo  vi machasaṃ  Dhitaraṃ madadahanatvāna Mekhalehi  machasaṃ  Gacchasi  machasaṃ Gayhāvako gacchati yena kāma  vi  Saceva ajjadhāresi  machasaṃ Bhariṃsu  machasaṃ  Kañajaroca nikujati  vi machasaṃ syā Anupathe  machasaṃ  Asso hasisati dvāre kumāro uparodatiKhattiyānaṃ kule bhadde kinnu sukhataraṃ tato Mayurakoñcāhirude kokilābhinikujiteKhantiyānaṃ kule bhadde kinnu sukhataraṃ tato  Kahaṃ nukho sattumaddano pararaṭṭhappamaddanoKuso soḷārapaññāṇo so no dukkhā pamocaye Idheva so sattumaddano  pararaṭṭhappamaddanoKuso soḷārapaññāṇo yo no dukkhā  pamocaye Ummattikā nu bhanasi ādu bālāva  bhāsasiKuso ce āgato assa kiṃ na jānemu taṃ mayaṃ  Eso āḷāriko poso kumāripuramantareDaḷhaṃ katvāna saṃvelliṃ  kumbhiṃ dhovati onato Veṇi tvamasi caṇḍāli ādusi kulagandhinīKathaṃ maddakule jātā dasaṃ kayirāsi kāmukaṃ Nambhi veṇi na vaṇḍāli na cambhi kulagandhinīOkkākaputto bhaddante tvannu dāsoti maññasi Yo brāhmaṇasahassāni sadā bhojeti visatiṃOkkākaputto bhaddante tvannu dāsoti maññasi  Yassa nāgasahassāni sadā bhojenti visatiṃOkkākaputto bhaddante tvannu dāsoti maññasi Sattumadāno  machasaṃ  Sabbe vadhissati  machasaṃ  Andhabālā  machasaṃAndhabālā pabhāssi  syā  Saṃvellaṃ  machasaṃ syā  Yassa assasahassāni sadā bhojenti visatiṃOkkākaputto bhaddante tvannu dāsoti maññasi Yassa rathasahassāni sadā yojenti visatiṃOkkākaputto bhaddante tvannu dāsoti maññasi Yassa usabhasasahassāni sadā yojenti visatiṃOkkākaputto bhaddante tvannu dāsoti maññasi Yassa dhenusahassāni sadā dughanti  visatiṃOkkākaputto bhaddante tvannu dāsoti maññasi Taggha te dukkaṭaṃ bale yaṃ khattiyaṃ mahabbalaṃNāgaṃ maṇḍukavaṇṇe na taṃ akkhāsi āgataṃ  Aparādhaṃ mahārāja tvaṃ no khama rathesabhaYaṃ taṃ aññātavesena naññāsimbhā idhāgataṃ Mādisassa na taṃ channaṃ yohaṃ aḷāriko bhaveTvaññeva me pasidassu nanthi te deva dukkaṭaṃ  Gaccha bale khamāpehi kusarājaṃ mahabbalaṃKhamāpito kusarājā so te dassati jīvitaṃ Pitussa vacanaṃ sutvā devavaṇṇi pabhāvatīSirasā aggahi pāde kusarājaṃ mahabbalaṃ Yā imā ratyo atikkantā tā imā deva tayā vināVande te sirasā pāde mā me kujjha rathesabha Saccaṃ te  paṭijānāmi mahārāja suṇohi meNa cāpi appiyaṃ  tuyhaṃ kareyyāmi ahaṃ puna Duhanti  machasaṃ vi syā  Nanaṃ ākkhāsimāgataṃ  machasaṃ syā Sabbaṃ te  machasaṃ  Apiyaṃ  machasaṃ  Evañce yāvamānāya vacanaṃ me na kāhasiIdāni maṃ tāto havatvā khantiyānaṃ padasasti Evante yācamānāya kiṃ na kāhāmi te vacoVikuddho tyasmi kalyāṇi mā tvaṃ bhāyi pabhāvati  Saccante paṭijānāmi rājaputti suṇohi meNa cāpi appiyaṃ tuyhaṃ kareyyāmi ahaṃ puna Taca kāmā hi sussoṇi bahuṃ dukkhaṃ titikkhisaṃPahu maddakulaṃ gantvā nayituṃ taṃ pabhāvati Yojayantu rathe asse nānācitte samāhiteAtha dakkhatha me vegaṃ vidhamentassa sattavo Tañca tattha udikkhiṃsu rañño maddassa thipure Vijambhamānaṃ sīhaṃva pothentaṃ diguṇaṃ bhujaṃ  Hatthakkhandhañca āruyha āropetvā pabhavatiṃSaṅgāmaṃ otaritvāna sihanādaṃ nadi kuso Tassa taṃ nadato sutvā sihassevitare migāKhantiyā vipalāyiṃsu kusaddasabhayaṭṭitā Hatthārohā anikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakāAññamaññassa chindanti kusasaddabhayaṭṭitā Tasmiṃ saṅghāmasisassamiṃ passitvā tuṭṭhamānaso Kusassa rañño devindo adā verocanaṃ maṇi So taṃ vijitvā saṅgāmaṃ laddhā verocanaṃ maṇiṃHatthikkhandhagato rājā pāvekkhi nagaraṃ puraṃ Jivagāhaṃ  gahetvāna bandhitvā satta khattiyeSasurassupanāmesi ime te deva sattavo Maddasasante pure  machasaṃ  Haṭṭhamānaso  vi machasaṃ  Jivaggāhaṃ machasaṃ      Sabbeva te vasaṅgatā amittā vihatā tacaKāmaṃ karohi te tayā muñca vā te hanassu vā  Tumbheva  sattavo ete nahi te myaha sattavoTvaññeva no mahārāja muñca vā te hanassu vā Imā te dhītaro satta devakaññupamā subhāDadāhi nesaṃ ekekaṃ hontu jāmātaro taca Ambhākañceva tvaṃ no sabbesamissaroTvaññeva no mahārāja dehi nesaṃ yadicchasi Ekamekasasa ekekaṃ adā sihassaro kusoKhattiyānaṃ tadā nesaṃ rañño maddassa dhitaro Piṇitā  tena lābhena tuṭṭhā sihasasare kuseSakaraṭṭhāni pāyiṃsu khattiyā satta tāvade Pabhāvatiñca ādāya maṇiṃ verocanaṃ subhaṃKusāvatiṃ kuso rājā agamāsi mahabbalo Tyassu ekarathe yantā pavisantā kusāvatiṃ Samānā vaṇṇarūpena nāññamaññamatirocayuṃ  Mātā puttena saṅgañachi ubhayo ca jayampatīSamaggā te tadā āsuṃ phītaṃ dharaṇimāvasunti Kusajātakaṃ Tuyheva  vi machasaṃ syā  Paṇitā  vi machasaṃ  Rocayiṃsu  machasaṃ  Soṇanandajātakaṃ  Devatānusi gandhabbo ādu sakko purindadoManussabhuto iddhimā kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ Namhi devo na gandhabbo namhi sakko purindadoManussabhuto iddhimā evaṃ jānāhi bhārata  Katarūpamidaṃ bhotā  veyyāvaccaṃ anappakaṃDevambhi vassamānambhi anovassaṃ bhavaṃ akā Tato vātātape ḷore sitacchāyaṃ bhavaṃ akāTato amittamajjhe  ca saratāṇaṃ bhavaṃ akā Tato phitāni raṭṭhāni vasino te bhavaṃ akāTato ekasataṃ khatye anuyante bhavaṃ akā Patitāssu  mayaṃ bhoto vara taṃ bhaññamicchasi Hatthiyānaṃ assarathaṃ nāriyo ca alaṅkatāNivesanāni rammāni mayaṃ bhoto dadāmase Atha vā aṅge vā magadhe  mayaṃ bhoto dadāmaseAtha vā assakāvantiṃ sumanā damma te mayaṃ Upaḍḍhaṃ vāpi rajjassa mayaṃ bhoto dadāmaseSace te attho rajjena anusāsa yadicchasi  Na me atthopi rājjena nagarena dhanena vāAthopi janapadena attho mayhaṃ na vijjati Bhotova raṭṭhe vijite araññe atthi assamoPitā mayhaṃ janetti ca ubho sammanti assame Tesāhaṃ pubbācariyesu puññaṃ na labhāmi  kātaveBhavantaṃ ajjhācaraṃ katvā soṇaṃ yācāmu  saṃvaraṃ Bhāradha  machasaṃ  Bhoto  syā  Amittamajjhesu  machasaṃ syā Patitassu  machasaṃ  Vadataṃbhuñajamicchasi  machasaṃ  Athavaṅgavā magadhe machasaṃ syā  Labbhāmi  machasaṃ  Yāmecu  machasaṃ  Karomi te taṃ vacanaṃ yaṃ maṃ bhaṇasi brāhmaṇaEtañca kho no akkhāhi nivanto hontu yācakā  Parosataṃ jānapadā  mahāsālā ca brāhmaṇāIme ca khattiyā sabbe abhijātā yasassinoBhavañca rājā manojo alaṃ hessanti yācakā Hatthi asse ca yojentu rathaṃ santayha sārathiĀbandhanāni gaṇhatha pādesussārayaṃ dajeAssamaṃ taṃ gamissāmi yattha sammani kosiyo Tato ca rājā pāyāsi senāya caturaṅginiAgamāsi  assamaṃ rammaṃ yattha sammati kosiyo  Kassa kādambayo  kājo vehāsaṃ caturaṅgulaṃAṃsaṃ asamphusaṃ eti udabhārasasa gacchato Ahaṃ soṇo mahārāja tāpaso sahitabbatoBharāmi mātāpitaro rattindivamatandito Vane phalañca mulañca āharitvā disampatiPosemi mātāpitaro pubbekatamanussaraṃ  Icchāmi assamaṃ gantuṃ yattha sammati kosiyoMaggaṃ no soṇa akkhāhi yena gacchemu assamaṃ Ayaṃ ekapadi rāja yenetaṃ meghasantihaṃAkoviḷārehi sañachannaṃ ettha sammati kosiyo Idaṃ vatvāna pakkāmi taramāno mahāisiVehāse antalikkhasmiṃ anusāsitvāna khattiye Assamaṃ parimajjitvā paññāpetvāna āsanaṃPaṇṇasālaṃ pavisitvā pitaraṃ paṭibodhayi Janapadā  vi machasaṃ  Agāmā  vi Machasaṃ  Kādambamayo  machasaṃ  Ime āyanti rājāno abhijātā yasassinoAssamā nikkhamitvāna nisidāhi  mahāisi Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā taramāno mahāisiAssamā nikkhamitvāna padvārambhi upāvisi Tañca disvāna āyantaṃ jalantariva tejasāKhatti  saṅghaparibbuḷhaṃ kosiyo etadabravi Kassa bherī mudiṅgā ca saṅkhā paṇavadeṇḍimā Purato viṭapantāni hāsayantā rathesabhaṃ Kassa kañcanapaṭṭena puthunā vijjuvaṇṇināYuvā kalāpasannaddho ko eti siriyā jalaṃ Ukkā mukhe  pahaṭṭhaṃva khadiraṅgārasantibhaṃMukhañca ruciraṃ bhāti ko eti siriyā jalaṃ Tassa pagaghitaṃ chattaṃ sasalākaṃ manoramaṃĀdiccaraṃsāvaraṇaṃ  ko eti siriyā jalaṃ Kassa aṅgaṃ pariggayha vālavijanimuttamāCaranti varapaññassa  hatthikkhandhena āyato Kassa setāni chattāni ājāniyā ca vammitā Samantā parikiranti ko eti siriyā jalaṃ Kassa ekasataṃ khatyā anuyantā yasassinoSamantā anupariyanti ko eti siriyā jalaṃ Hatthi assā rathā patti senāya caturaṅganīSamantā anupariyanti ko eti siriyā jalaṃ Kassesā mahati senā piṭṭhito anuvatattīAkkhobhanī apariyantā sāgarasseva ūmiyo Nisada tvaṃ mahā ise  vi machasaṃ syā  Khatya  machasaṃ Nindimā  machasaṃ  Mukhaṃ  machasaṃ  Ādicca rasāvaraṇaṃ  machasaṃ Varapuññassa  machasaṃ  Camimikā  machasaṃ      Rājābhirājā manojo indeva jayataṃ pati nandassajjhāvaraṃ eti assamaṃ brahmacārinaṃ Tassesā mahati senā piṭṭhito anuvattatiAkkhobhani apariyantā sāgarasseva ūmiyo  Anulittā candanena kāsikuttamadhārinoSabbe pañajalikā hutvā isinaṃ ajjhupāgamuṃ Kacci nu bhoto kusalaṃ kacci bhoto anāmayaṃKacci uñechana yāpetha kacci mulaphalā bahu Kacci ḍaṃsā ca makasā appameva siriṃsapāVane vālamigākiṇṇe kacci hiṃsā na vijjati Kusalañce no rāja atho rāja anāmayaṃAtho uñechana yāpema atho mulaphalā bahu Atho ḍaṃsā ca makasā appameva siraṃsapā Vane vālamigākiṇṇe hiṃsā ambhaṃ  na vijjati Bahuni vassapugāni assame vasato  idhaNābhijānāmi uppannaṃ ābādhaṃ amanoramaṃ Svāgatante mahārāja atho te adurāgataṃIssarosi anuppatto yaṃ idhatthi pavedayaṃ   Tindukāni  piyālāni madhuke kāsa  māriyoPhalāni khuddakappāni bhuñja rāja varaṃ varaṃ Idampi pāniyaṃ sītaṃ ābhataṃ girigababharāTato piva mahārāja sace tvaṃ abhikaṅkhasi Paṭiggahitaṃ yaṃ dinnaṃ sabbassa agghiyaṃ kataṃNandassāpi nisāmetha vacanaṃ yaṃ  pavakkhati Sarisapā  machasaṃ  Mayhaṃ  machasaṃ  Samamato  machasaṃ sammataṃ  vi Pavedhaya  machasaṃ  Tiṇḍukāni  machasaṃ  Kāsu  vi machasaṃ  So  machasaṃ  Ajjhavarambhā nandassa bhoto santikamāgatāSuṇātu me bhavaṃ vacanaṃ nandassa parisāya ca Parosataṃ jānapadā mahāsālā ca brāhmaṇāIme ca khattiyā sabbe abhijātā yasassinoBhavañca rājā manojo anumaññantu me vaco Ye vasanti samitāro yakkhāni idha asasameAraññe bhūtabhavyāni suṇantu vacanaṃ mama Namo katvāna bhūtānaṃ isiṃ vakkhāmi subbataṃSo tyāhaṃ dakkhiṇo  bāhu tava kosiya sammato Pitaraṃ me janettiñca bhattukāmassa me satoVīra puññamidaṃ ṭhānaṃ mā maṃ kosiya vāraya  Sabbhihetaṃ upaññātaṃ mametaṃ apanissajaUṭṭhānapāricariyāya dīgharattaṃ tayā kataṃMātāpitusu puññāni mama lokadado bhava Tatheva santi manujā dhamme dhammapadaṃ vudu Maggo saggassa lokassa yathā jānāsi tvaṃ ise Uṭṭhānapāricariyāya mātāpitu sukhāvahaṃTaṃ maṃ puññābhivāreti ariyamaggāvaro naro  Suṇantu bhonto vacanaṃ bhātu  rajjhāvarā mamaKulavaṃsaṃ mahārāja porāṇaṃ parihāpayaṃAdhammacāri  yo jeṭṭho nirayaṃ so upapajjati Dakkhiṇaṃ  machasaṃ  Vida  machasaṃ  Bhāta  vi machasaṃ  Adhammacārijeṭṭhesu  machasaṃ syā adhacāri jeṭṭho  vi  Ye ca dhammassa kusalā porāṇassa disampatiCārintena ca sampannā na te gacchanti duggatiṃ Mātāpitā ca bhātā ca bhagini ñātibandhavāSabbe jeṭṭhassa te bhārā evaṃ jānāhi bhārata  Ādiyitvā garuṃ bhāraṃ nāviko viya ussaheDhammañca nappamajjāmi  jeṭṭhocasmi rathesabha Adhigatambhā  tame ñāṇaṃ jālaṃva jātavedato Evameva no bhavaṃ dhammaṃ kosiyo pavidaṃsayi Yathā udayamādicco vāsudevo pabhaṅkaroPāṇinaṃ pavidaṃseti rūpaṃ kalyāṇapāpakaṃEvameva no bhavaṃ dhammaṃ kosiyo pavidaṃsayi  Evaṃ me yācamānassa añjaliṃ nāvakhujjhathaTava baddhacaro  hessaṃ vuṭṭhito paricārako  Addhā nanda pajānāsi saddhammaṃ sabbhi desitaṃAriyo ariyasamācāro bāḷhaṃ tvaṃ mama ruccasi Bhavantaṃ vadāmi bhotiñca suṇātha vacanaṃ mamaNāyaṃ bhāro bhāramatto ahu mayhaṃ kudācanaṃ Bhāradha  machasaṃ  Pamajjāmina  machasaṃ  Adhigamā  machasaṃ adhigamahā syā  Jātavedaso  machasaṃ  Tavupaṭṭhacaro  machasaṃ tavapaṭṭhavaro syā Paricāriko  machasaṃ  Taṃ maṃ upaṭṭhitaṃ santaṃ mātāpitu sukhāvahaṃNando ajjhācaraṃ katvā upaṭṭhānāya yācati  Yo ce icchati kāmena santānaṃ brahmacārinaṃNandaṃ vo caratha eko kaṃ nando upatiṭṭhatu Tayā tāta anuññātā soṇa taṃ nissitā mayaṃUpaghāyituṃ  labhe nandaṃ muddhani brahmacārinaṃ Assatthasseva taruṇaṃ pavāḷaṃ māḷuteritaṃCirassa nandaṃ disvāna hadayaṃ me pavedhati Yadā suttāpi supine  nandaṃ passāmi āgataṃUdaggā sumanā homi nando no āgato ayaṃ Yadā ca paṭikhujjhitvā nandaṃ passāmi nāgataṃBhiyo  āvisati soko domanassañcanappakaṃ  Sāhaṃ ajja cirassampi nandaṃ passāmi āgataṃBhattu ca mayhañca piyo nando no pāvisi gharaṃ Pitu ca  nando suppiyo  yaṃ nando nappavase gharā Labhatu tāta nando taṃ maṃ nando upatiṭṭhatu Anukampikā patiṭṭhā ca pubbe rasadadi ca noMaggo saggassa lokassa mātā taṃ varate ise Pubbe rasadadi gonti mātā puññupasañahitāMaggo saggassa lokassa mātā taṃ varate ise  Ākakkhamānā puttaphalaṃ devatāya namassati nakkhantāni ca pucchatiutusaṃvaccharāni ca Tassā atusinātāya hoti gabbhassavakkamo Tena dohaḷini hoti suhadā tena vuccati Upaghātuṃ  machasaṃ syā  Suppanne  machasaṃ syā Hiyo  machasaṃ  Pitupi  vi machasaṃ  Supiyo  machasaṃ Gharaṃ  machasaṃ syā  Anukamapakā  machasaṃ syā Vokkamo  vi machasaṃ  Saṃvaccharaṃ vā ūnaṃ vā pariharitvā vijāyatiTena sā janayantiti janetti tena vuccati Thanakkhirena gitena aṅgapāpūraṇena caRodantaṃ puttaṃ toseti  tosenti tena vuccati Tato vātātape ghore mamaṃ  katvā udikkhatiDārakaṃ appajānantaṃ  posenti tena vuccati Yañca mātu dhanaṃ hoti yaññaca hoti pituddhanaṃUbhayampetassa gopeti api puttassa no siyāEvaṃ puttaṃ aduṃ putta iti mātā vihaññati Pamattaṃ paradāresu nisithe  pattayobbaneSāyaṃ puttaṃ anāyantaṃ iti matā vihaññati Evaṃ kicchā bhato poso mātu aparivārakoMātarī micchā caritvāna nirayaṃ so upapajjati Evaṃ kicchā bhato poso pitu aparivārakoMātaraṃ aparicaritvāna kicchaṃ vā so upapajjati Dhanāpi  dhanakāmānaṃ nassati iti me sutaṃMātaraṃ aparicaritvāna kicchaṃ vā so nigacchati Dhanāpi dhanakāmānaṃ nassati iti me sutaṃPitaraṃ aparicaritvāna kicchaṃ vā so nigacchati Ānando ca pamādo ca sadā hasitakīḷitaṃMātaraṃ paricaritvāna labbhametaṃ  vijānato Tosenti  vi machasaṃ  Mammaṃ  machasaṃ mamiṃ  vi  Apajānattaṃ  vi machasaṃ Niside  machasaṃ nissive  syā  Aparicāriko  machasaṃ Dhanaṃpi  machasaṃ syā  Labbatena  machasaṃ syā      Ānando ca pamādo ca sadā hasitakīḷitaṃPītaraṃ paricaritvāna labbhametaṃ vijānato Dānañca piyavācā ca atthacariyā ca yā idhaSamānattatā ca dhammesu tattha tattha yathārahaṃ Ete kho saṃgahā loke rathassāṇiva yāyatoEte ca saṅghahā nāssu na mātā puttakāraṇāUabhetha mānaṃ pūjaṃ vā pitā vā puttakāraṇā  Yasmā ca saṅgahā  ete samavekkhanti paṇḍitāTsamā mahantaṃ papponti pāsaṃsā  ca bhavanti te Brahmamāti mātāpitaro pubbācariyāti vuccareĀhunaiyyā ca puttānaṃ pajāya anukampakā Tasmā hi te namasseyya sakkareyyātha  paṇḍitoAnnena atho pānena vatthena sayanena caUcchādanena nahāpanne pādānaṃ dhovanena ca Tāya naṃ pāricariyāya mātāpitusu paṇḍitā Idheva  pasaṃsanti pecca sagge pamodatiti SoṇanandajātakaṃSattatinipāto niṭṭhitoTassuddānaṃAtha sattatimmahi nipātavareSa bhavaṃ tu kusāvati rājavaroAtha soṇanandavaro ca punaAbhivāsita sattatimambhi suteti Saṅghahe  machasaṃ  Pasaṃsā  vi machasaṃ  Sakakareyyava  machasaṃ Paṇḍito  machasaṃ  Idhaceva  vi Asītinipāto Cullahaṃsajātakaṃ  Sumukha anupacinantā pakkamanti vibhaṅgamāGaccha tuvampi mā kaṅkhi natthi baddhe  sahāyatā Gacchevāhaṃ na vā gacche na tena amaro siyaṃSukhitaṃ taṃ upāsitvā sukkhitaṃ taṃ kathaṃ rahe Maraṇaṃ vā tayā saddhiṃ jīvitaṃ vā tayā vināTadeva maraṇaṃ seyyo yañce jive tayā vinā  Nesa dhammo mahārāja yaṃ taṃ evaṃ gataṃ  jaheYā gati tuyhaṃ sā mayhaṃ ruccate vihagādhipa  Kā nu pāsena baddhassa  gati aññā mahānasāSā kathaṃ cetayānassa muttassa tava ruccati Kaṃ vā tvaṃ passase atthaṃ mama tuyhañca pakkhimaÑātinaṃ vāvasiṭṭhānaṃ ubhintaṃ jīvitakkhaye Yaṃ nu kañcanadepiccha  andhena tamasā gataṃTādise sañcajaṃ pāṇaṃ kamatthamahijotaye Kathannu patataṃ seṭṭha dhamme atthaṃ na khujjhaseDhammo apavito santo atthaṃ dasseti pāṇinaṃ      ra Sohaṃ dhammaṃ avekkhanto dhammā catthaṃ samuṭṭhitaṃBhattiñca tayi sampassaṃ nāvakaṅkhāmi jivataṃ Addhā eso sataṃ dhammo yo mitetā mittamāpadeNaccaje jīvitasasāpi hetu dhammaṃ anussaraṃ Svāyaṃ dhamemā ca te ciṇṇo hatti ca viditā mayiKāmaṃ karassu mayhetaṃ gacchevānumato mayā Natthi bandhe  machasaṃ  Kataṃ  machasaṃ  Vihaṅgādhipa  machasaṃ  Bandhassa machasaṃ  Cepiñcha  machasaṃ  Ayaṃ gāthā pādo maramma potthakesu na disasti  Api tvevaṃ gate kāle yaṃ baddhaṃ ñātinaṃ mayāTayā taṃ buddhisampanna assa paramaṃvutaṃ Iccevaṃ mantayantānaṃ ariyānaṃ ariyavuttinaṃPaccadissatha nesādo āturānamivantako Te sattuṃ abhisaṃcikkha digharattaṃ hitā dijāTuṇhimāsittha ubhayo na ca sañcesumāsanā Dhataraṭṭhe ca disvāna samuḍḍhente tato tatoAbhikkamatha vegena dvijasattu dvijādhipe So ca vegenabhikkamma āsajja parame dijePaccakampittha nesādo baddhā iti vicintayaṃ Ekañca baddhimāsinaṃ abaddhañca punāparaṃĀsajja baddhamāsinaṃ pekkhamānamadinavaṃ Tato so vimato yeva paṇḍare ajjhabhāsathaPavaddhakāye āsine dijasaṅghagaṇādhipe Yannu pāsena mahatā baddho na kurute disaṃAtha kasmā abaddho tvaṃ bali pakkhī na gacchasi Kinnu tāyaṃ dijo hoti mutto baddhaṃ upāsasiOhāya sakuṇā yanti kiṃ eko avahiyasi Rājā meso dijāmitta sakhā pāṇasamo ca meNeva naṃ vijahissāmi yāva kālassa pariyāyaṃ  Kathaṃ panāyaṃ vihago nāddasā pāsamoḍḍitaṃPadaṃ hetaṃ mahantānaṃ boddhumarahanti āpadaṃ Yadā parābhavo hoti poso jīvitasaṅkayeAtha jālañca pāsañca āsājjapi na khujjhati Api tveva mahāpañña pāsā bahuvidhā tatāGulhamāsajja bajjhanti athevaṃ jīvitakkhaye   Apināyaṃ tayā saddhiṃ sambhāsassa sukhudrayoApi no anumaññasi api no jīvitaṃ dade Na ceva me tvaṃ baddhosi napi icchāmi te vadhaṃKāmaṃ khippamito gantvā jiva tvaṃ anigho ciraṃ Na vāhametaṃ  icchāmi aññatretassa jīvitāSace ekena tuṭṭhosi muñcetaṃ mañca bhakkhaya Ārohapariṇāhena tulyasmā vayasā ubhoNa te lābhena jinatthi  etena niminā tuvaṃ Tadiṅgha samavekkhassu hotu giddhi tavāsmasuMaṃ pubbe bandha pāsena pacchā muñca dijādhipaṃ Tāvadeva ca te lābho katassa yācanāya caMitti ca dhataraṭṭhehi yāvajivāya te siyā Passantu no mahāsaṅghā tayā muttaṃ ito gataṃMittāmaccā ca bhattā ca puttadārā ca bandhavā Na ca te tādisā mittā bahuntaṃ  idha vijjatiYathā tvaṃ dhataraṭṭhassa pāṇasādhāraṇo sakhā So te sahāyaṃ muñcāmi hotu rājā tavānugoKāmaṃ khippamito gantvā ñātimajjhe virocatha So patito pamuttena bhattunā bhattu gāravoAjjhabhāsatha vakkaṅgo vācaṃ kaṇṇasukhaṃ bhaṇaṃ Evaṃ luddaka nandassa saha sabbehi ñātihiYathāhamajja nandāmi muttaṃ disvā dijādhipaṃ Ehi taṃ anusikkhāmi yathā tuvampi lacchaseLābhaṃ yathāyaṃ  dhataraṭṭho pāpaṃ kiñci na dakkhati Khippamante puraṃ netvā  rañño dassehi no ubhoAbaddhe pakatībhute kāje ubhayate ṭhite Nevāhaṃ  machasaṃ  Jivatthi  machasaṃ  Bahunaṃ  machasaṃ  Tavāya machasaṃsyā  Gantvā  machasaṃ syā  Dhataraṭṭhā mahārāja haṃsādhipatino imeAyaṃ hi rājā haṃsānaṃ ayaṃ senāpatitaro Asaṃsayaṃ imaṃ disvā haṃsarājaṃ narādhipoPatitā sumano vitto bahuṃ dassati te dhanaṃ  Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā vihagā  tava hatthatthamāgatāKathaṃ luddo mahantānaṃ issaremidhamajjhagā Vihitā santi me pāsā pallalesu janādhipaYaṃ yadāyatanaṃ maññe dijānaṃ pāṇarodhanaṃ Tādisaṃ pāsamāsajja haṃsarājā abajjhathaTaṃ abaddho upāsino mamāyaṃ ajjhabhāsatha Sudukkaraṃ anariyehi dahate bhāvamuttamaṃBhatturatthe parakkanto dhamme yutto vihaṅgamo Attanāyaṃ cajitvāna jīvitaṃ jīvitārahoAnutthunanto āsino bhattu yācittha jīvitaṃ Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā pasādamahamajjhagaṃTato naṃ pāmuviṃ pāsā anuññāsiṃ sukhena ca So patito pamuttena battunā bhattugāracoAjjhaśasatha vakkaṅgo vācaṃ kaṇṇasukhaṃ bhaṇaṃ Kammamunā  machasaṃ syā  Vibhaṅga  machasaṃ syā  Evaṃ luddaka nandassu saha sabbehi ñātibhiYathāhamajja nandami muttaṃ disvā dijādhipaṃ Ehi taṃ anusikkhāmi yathā tvamapi lacchaseLābhaṃ yathāyaṃ dhataraṭṭho pāpaṃ kiñci nadakkhati  Khippamantepuraṃ gantvā rañño dassehi no ubhoAbaddhe pakatibhūte kāje uīyato ṭhite Dhataraṭṭhā mahārāja haṃsādhipatino imeAyaṃ hi rājā haṃsānaṃ ayaṃ senāpatitaro Asaṃsayaṃ imaṃ disvā haṃsarājaṃ narādhipoPatito sumano vitto bahuṃ dasasti te dhanaṃ  Evametassa vacanā ānitāme ubho mayāEttheva hi ime assu ubho anumatā mayā Soyaṃ evaṃ gato pakkhī dijo paramadhammikoMādisassa hi luddassa janayeyyātha maddavaṃ Upāyanaṃ hi  te deva nāññaṃ passāmi edisaṃSabbasākuṇikagāme taṃ passa manujādhipa  Disvā nisinnaṃ rājānaṃ piṭhe sovaṇṇaye subheAjjhabhāsatha vakkaṅgo vācaṃ kaṇṇasukhaṃ bhaṇaṃ Kaccinu bhoto kusalaṃ kacci bhoto anāmayaṃKacci raṭṭhamidaṃ phītaṃ dhammena manusisasati  Kusalañceva me haṃsa atho haṃsa anāmayaṃAtho raṭṭhamidaṃ phītaṃ dhammena manusisasti Kacci bhoto amaccesu doso koci na vijjatiKaccinnu te tavatthesu nāvakaṅkhanti jīvitaṃ Athopi me amaccesu doso koci na vijjatiAtho te mamatthesu nāvakaṅkhanti jīvitaṃ Nadakkhasi  machasaṃ  Ca  machasaṃ  Manusāsati  machasaṃ syā      Kacci te sādisi bhariyā assavā piyabhāṇiniPuttarūpayasupetā tava chandamasānugā Atho me sādisi bhariyā assavā piyyāṇinīPuttarūpayasupetā mama chandavasānugā  Bhavaṃ tu kacci nu mahāsattuhatthatthataṅgatoDukkhamāpajji vipulaṃ tasmiṃ paṭhamamāpade Kacciyaṃ  nāpatitvāna daṇejena samapoṭhayiEvametesaṃ jamamānaṃ pākatikaṃ bhavati tāvade Khemamāsi mahārāja evamāpadi  saṃsatiNa cāyaṃ kiñcirasmāsu satatuva samapajjatha  Paccakampittha nesādo pubbeva ajjhabhāsathaTadāyaṃ sumukhoyeva paṇḍito paccahāsatha  Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā pasādamayamajjhagā tato maṃ pāmuci pāsā anuññāsi sukenaca Idampi sumukheneva etadatthāya cintitaṃBhoto sakāse āgamanaṃ etassa dhanamicchatā Svāgatañcevidaṃ bhavataṃ patitocasmi dassanāEso api bahuṃ vittaṃ labhataṃ yāvaticchati  Santappayitvā nesādaṃ bhogehi manujādhipoAjjhabhāsatha vakkaṅgaṃ  vācaṃ kaṇṇasukhaṃ bhaṇaṃ Yaṃ balu dhammadhinaṃ  vaso vattati kiñcanaṃSabbatthissariyaṃ  bhavataṃ pasāsatha  yadicchatha Dānatthaṃ upabhottuṃ vā yañcaññaṃ upakappatiEtaṃ dadāmi vo vitataṃ isseraṃ vissajāmi vo  Yathā ca myāyaṃ sumukho ajjhabhāseyya paṇḍitoKāmasā khuddhisampanno taṃ myāssa paramappiyaṃ Kacciyanto  machasaṃ  Vakkaṅgo  machasaṃ syā Evamāpariyāsati  syā  Dhamammādhinaṃ  machasaṃ syāEvamāpadiyāsati  machasaṃ  Sababissariyaṃ  machasaṃ Māpajjatha  machasaṃ  Taṃ pasāsaṃ  machasaṃ Ajjhabhāsatha  machasaṃ  Ahaṃ balu mahārāja nāgarājārivantaraṃPaṭivattuṃ na sakkomi na me so vinayo siyā Ambhākañceva yo seṭṭho tvañca uttamasattavoBhumipālo manusasindo pujā bahuhi hetuhi Tesaṃ abhinnaṃ bhaṇataṃ vattamāne vinicchayeNāntaraṃ  paṭivattabbaṃ pesesna  manujādhipa Dhamemana kira nesādo paṇḍito aṇḍajo itiNaheva akatattassa nayo etādiso siyā Evaṃ aggapakatimā evaṃ uttamasatatavoYāvatatthi mayā diṭṭhā nāññaṃ passāmi edisaṃ Tuṭṭhosmi co pakatiyā vākeyyana madhurena caEso cāpi mama chando ciraṃ passeyya vo ubho  Yaṃ kiccaṃ parame mitte katarasmāsu  taṃ tayāPattā nissaṃsayaṃ tyambhā bhattirasmāsu yā tava Aduñca nūna sumahā ñātisaṅghassamantaraṃAdasasanena asmākaṃ dukkhaṃ bahūsu pakkhisu Tesaṃ sokavighātāya tayā anumatā mayaṃTaṃ padakkhiṇato katvā ñāti passe marindama  Addhāhaṃ vipulaṃ pitiṃ bhavataṃ vindāmi dassanāEso cāpi mahā attho ñātivissāsanā siyā  Idaṃ vatvā dhataraṭṭhā  haṃsarājā narādhipaṃUttamajavamattāya ñātisaṅghamupāgamuṃ Te aroge anuppatte disvāna parame dvijeKekānimakaruṃ haṃsā puthu paddo ajāyatha Nattaraṃ  machasaṃ syā  Pesena  machasaṃ  Katimasmāsu  machasaṃ Murindama  machasaṃ syā  Dhataraṭṭho  vi machasaṃ syā  Te patitā pamuttena bhattunā bhattugāravāSamantā parikariṃsu aṇḍajā laddhapaccayā Evaṃ mittavataṃ atthā sabbe honti padakkhiṇāHaṃsā yathā dhataraṭṭhā ñātisaṅghamupāgamutti Cullahaṃsajātakaṃ Mahāhaṃsajātaṃ  Ete haṃsā pakkamanti vakkaṅgā bhayameritāBharittava hemavaṇṇa kāmaṃ sumukha pakkama Obhāya maṃ ñātigaṇā ekaṃ pāsavasaṃ gataṃAnapekkhamānā gacchanti kiṃ eko avahiyyasi Pateva patataṃ seṭṭha natthi baddhe  sahāyatāMā anīghāya hāpesi kāmaṃ sumukha pakkama  Nāhaṃ dukkhaparetoti  dhataraṭṭha tavaṃ jaheJīvitaṃ maraṇaṃ vā me tayā saddhiṃ bhavissati Nāhaṃ dukkhaparetoti dhataraṭṭha tavaṃ jaheNa maṃ anariyasaṃyutte kamme yojetumarahasi Sakumāro sakhātyasami sacitte casamiṃ te ṭhitoÑāto senāpati tyāhaṃ saṃsānaṃ pavaruttama Kathaṃ ahaṃ vikatthissaṃ  ñātimajjhe ito gatoTaṃ hitvā patataṃ seṭṭha kinte vakkhāmito gatoIdha paṇaṃ cajissāmi nānariyaṃ kattumusasahe Eso hi dhammo sumukha yaṃ tvaṃ ariyapathe ṭhitoYo bhattāraṃ sakhāraṃ maṃ na pariccattumusasahe  Bandhe  machasaṃ syā  Pi  machasaṃ syā  Tuvaṃ  machasaṃ syā Vintisasaṃ  machasaṃ  Paridattu  machasaṃ   Taṃ hi me pekkhamānassa bhayaṃ na tveva jāyatiAdhigacchasi tvaṃ mayhaṃ evambhūtassa jīvitaṃ Icceva mantayantānaṃ ariyānaṃ ariyavuttinaṃDaṇḍamādāya nesādo āpadi  turito bhusaṃ Tamāpatantaṃ disvāna sumukho apari  brūhayiAṭṭhāsi purato rañño haṃso vissāsayaṃ vyathaṃ  Mā bhāyi pattaṃ seṭṭha nahi bhāyanati tādisāAhaṃ yogaṃ payuñachayasaṃ yuttaṃ dhammupasaṃhitaṃTena pariyāpadānena  khippaṃ pāsā pamokkhasi  Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā sumukhassa subhāsitaṃPahaṭṭhalomo nesādo añajalissa paṇāmayi Na me sutaṃ vā diṭṭhaṃ vā bhāsanto mānusiṃ dijoAriyaṃ bruvāno  vakkaṅgo cajanto mānusiṃ giraṃ Kinnu tāyaṃ dijo hoti mutto baddhaṃ  upāsasiObhāya sakuṇā yanati kiṃ eko avahiyasi  Rājā me so dijāmitta senāpaccassa kārayiṃTamāpade pariccattuṃ nussabhe vihagādipaṃ Mahāgaṇāya bhattā me me eko vyasanaṃ agāCajāmi taṃ samma nesāda bhattāyaṃ abhito rame Ariyavattasi cakkaṅga yo piṇḍamapacāyasiCajāmi te taṃ bhattāraṃ gacchathubho yathā sukhaṃ  Sace attappayogena ohito haṃsapakkhinaṃAnissaro muñcamambhe theyyaṃ kayirāsi luddaka Āpati  machasaṃ syā  Ati  machasaṃ syā  Byadhaṃ  machasaṃ Pariyādānena  machasaṃ  Mānusaṃ  machasaṃ  Bruhanto  vi machasaṃ syā Bandhaṃ  machasaṃ syā  Paṭiggaṇhama  machasaṃPiṭavu   Yassa tvaṃ batako  rañño kāmaṃ tasseva pāpayaTattha saṃyamano rājā yathābhiññaṃ karissati Icceva vutto nesādo hemavaṇeṇa haritataceUbho hatthehi saṅgayha  pañajare ajjhavodahi  Te pañajaragate pakkhī ubho hassaravaṇṇineSumukhaṃ dhataraṭṭhañca luddo ādāya pakkami Bhariyamāno dhataraṭṭho sumukhaṃ etadabuviKhāḷhaṃ bhāyāmi sumukha sāmāya lakkhaṇuruyāAsmākaṃ vadhamaññāya athattānaṃ vadhissati Pākahaṃsā ca sumukha suhemā hemasuttavāKoñca samuddatireva kapaṇā nūna rucchati Evaṃ mahanto lokassa appameyyo mahāgaṇiEkitthimanusoceyya na idaṃ paññavakomiva Vāto ca gandhamādeti ubhayaṃ chekapāpakaṃBālo āmakapakakaṃ ca lolo andho va āmisaṃ  Avinicchayaññu atthesu mandova paṭibhāsi  maṃKiccākiccaṃ na jānāsi sampatto kālapariyāyaṃ Aḍḍhummatto udiresi yo seyyā maññasitthiyoBahusādhāraṇā hetā soṇḍānaṃva surāgharaṃ Bhaṭako  machasaṃ  Paggayha  machasaṃ syā  Paṭibhāti  machasaṃ  Māyā cesā marici ca soko rogo vupaddavoKharā ca bandhanā cetā maccupāso guhāsayoTāsu yo visasase poso so naresu narādhamo  Yaṃ vuddhehi upaññātaṃ ko taṃ ninditumarahatiMahābhūtitthiyo nāma lokasmiṃ udapajjisuṃ Khiḍḍā paṇihitā tyāsu rati tyāsu patiṭṭhitāKhijāni tyāsu rūhanti yadidaṃ sattā pajāyareTāsu ko nibbide poso pāṇamāsajja pāṇihi Tvameva nañño sumukha thinaṃ atthesu yuñajasi tassa tyājja bhaye jāte bhītenajāyate mati Sabbo hi saṃsayaṃ patto bhayaṃ bhīrū titikkhatiPaṇḍitā ca mahattāno attho yuñajanti duyyuje Etadatthāya rājāno suramicchanti mantinaṃPaṭibāhati yaṃ suro āpadaṃ attapariyāyaṃ Mā no ajja vikantiṃsu rañño sudā mahānaseTathāhi vaṇṇo pattānaṃ phalaṃ veḷuṃva taṃ vadhi Mutto na icchi oḍḍetuṃ bandhaṃ upāgamiSopajja saṃsayaṃ patto atthaṃ gaṇhihi mā mukhaṃ Buddhehi  machasaṃ   So taṃ yogaṃ payujañassu yuttaṃ dhammupasaṃhataṃTavaṃ pariyāpadānena  mama pāṇesanaṃ cara  Mābhāyi patataṃ seṭṭha nahi bhāyanti tādisāAhaṃ yogaṃ payuñajissaṃ yuttaṃ dhammupasaṃhitaṃMama pariyāpadānena khippaṃ pāsā pamokkhasi Sa luddo haṃsakājena rājadvāraṃ upāgamiPaṭivedetha maṃ rañño dhataraṭṭhāyamāgato Te disavā puññasaṅkāse ubho lakkhaññasammateKhalu saññamano rājā amacce ajjhahāsatha Detha luddassa vatthāni attaṃ pānañca bhojanaṃthaKāmaṃ karo hiraññassa yāvanto esa icchati  Disvā luddaṃ pasantantaṃ kāsirājā tadābraviYadāyaṃ samma khemaka puṇṇā haṃsehi tiṭṭhati Kathaṃ ruciṃ majjhagataṃ pāsahattho upāgamiOkiṇṇaṃ ñātisaṅghehi nimajjhimaṃ kathaṃ gahi Ajja me sattamā ratti ādānāni upasato padametassa atvesaṃ appamatto Athassa padamaddakkhiṃ carato adanesanaṃTatthāhaṃ odahiṃ pāsaṃ evetaṃ dijamaggahiṃ  Ludda dve ime sakuṇā atha ekoti bhāsasiCittannu te vipariyattaṃ ādu kinnu jigiṃsasi  Yassa lohitakā tāḷā tapaneyyanibhā subhā Uraṃ saṃhacca tiṭṭhanti so me bandhaṃ upāgami Pariyādānena  machasaṃ  Saṃsamano  machasaṃ syā Kāsirājetadabruvi  machasaṃ syā  Ruci  machasaṃ syā Nimmajjhimaṃ  machasaṃ syā  Adanāni  machasaṃ Evaṃ taṃ  machasaṃ syā  Jigisati  machasaṃ  Sabhā  machasaṃ  Athāyaṃ bhassaro pakkhī abaddho baddhamāturaṃAriyaṃ bruvāno aṭṭhāsi vajanto mānusiṃ giraṃ  Atha ninnudāni sumukha hanuṃ saṃhacca tiṭṭhasiĀdu me parisaṃ patto bhayā bhito na bhāsasi Nāhaṃ kāsipati bhīto ogayha parisaṃ tavaNāhaṃ bhayā na bhāsissaṃ vākyaṃ atthasmiṃ tādise Na te abhisaraṃ passe na rathe napi pattikeNāssa cammaṃva kīṭaṃ vā vammite ca dhanuggahe Na hiraññaṃ suvaṇṇaṃ vā nagaraṃ vā sumāpitaṃOkiṇṇaparikhaṃ duggaṃ daḷhamaṭṭālakoṭṭhakaṃYattha paviṭṭho sumukha bhāyitabbaṃ na bhāyasi  Na me abhisarenattho nagarena dhanena vāApathena pathaṃ yāma antalikkhe carā mayaṃ Sutāva paṇḍitā tyambhā nipuṇā atthacintakāBhāsematthavatiṃ vācaṃ saccevasasa patiṭṭhito Kiñca tuyhaṃ asaccassa anariyassa karissatiMusāvādissa luddassa bhaṇitampi subhāsitaṃ Taṃ brahmaṇānaṃ vacanā imaṃ khemiṃ  akārayiAbhayañca tayā ghuṭṭhaṃ imāyo dasadhā disā Ogayha te pokkharaṇiṃ vippasannodakaṃ suciṃPahutañcādanaṃ tattha abhiṃsācettha pakkhinaṃ Abandho bandha  machasaṃ  Kiṃ  machasaṃ  Parikakhaṃ  machasaṃ Khemaṃ  machasaṃ  Bahukaṃ khādanaṃ  machasaṃ pahutaṃ khādanaṃ  syā  Idaṃ sutvāna nigghosaṃ āgatambhā  tavantikeTe te baddhasmā pāsena etaṃ te bhāsitaṃ musā Musāvādaṃ purakkhatvā icchālohañca pāpakaṃ Ubhosandhiṃ atikkamma asātaṃupapajjati  Nāparajjhāma sumukha napi lobhā camaggahiṃSutā ca paṇḍitātyattha nipuṇāatthacintakā Appevatthavatiṃ vācaṃ vyākareyyuṃ idhāgatāTathā taṃ samma nesādo vutetā sumukha magaghi Neva bhītā kāsipati upanitasmiṃ jiviteBhāsematthivatiṃ vācaṃ sampattā kālapariyāyaṃ Yo migena migaṃ hatti pakkhiṃ vā pana pakkhināSutena vā sutaṃ kiṇe kiṃ anariyataraṃ tato Yo ca ariyarudaṃ bhāse anariyadhammamavassitoUbho so dhaṃsate lokā idhaceva parattha ca Na majjetha yasaṃ patto na vyathe pattasaṃsayaṃVāyametheva kiccesu saṃvare vivarāni ca  Ye vaddhā abbhatikkantā sampattā kālapariyāyaṃIdha dhammaṃ caritvāna evete  tidivaṃ gatā Idaṃ sutvā kāsipati dhammamattani pālayaDhataraṭṭhañca muñcāhi haṃsānaṃ pavaruttamaṃ Āharantudakaṃ pajjaṃ āsanañca mahārahaṃPañajarato pamokkhāmi dhataraṭṭhaṃ yasassinaṃ Agatamha  machasaṃ  Bandhasmā  vi machasaṃ  Bhūtā  machasaṃ syā Kiṇyā  machasaṃ kilyā  syā  Nabyādhe  machasaṃ syā  Vuḍḍānābabhatikkhantā machasaṃ  Evaṃ te  machasaṃ syā  Tañca senāpatiṃ dhiraṃ nipuṇaṃ atthacintakaṃYo sukho sukhino rañño dukkhite hoti dukkhito Etādisā kho arahanti piṇḍamasnātu bhattunoYathāyaṃ sumukho rañño pāṇasādhāraṇo sakhā  Pīṭhañca sababasovaṇṇaṃ aṭṭhapadaṃ manoramaṃMaṭṭhaṃ kāsikapatthinnaṃ dharaṭṭho upāvisi Kocchañca sabbasovaṇṇaṃ veyyagghaparisibbitaṃSumukho ajjhupāvekkhi dhataraṭṭhassa anantaraṃ Tesaṃ kañcanapattehi puthu ādāya kāsiyoBhaṃsānaṃ abhihāresu aggaṃ rañño pavāsitaṃ Disvā abhihaṭaṃ aggaṃ kāsirājena pesitaṃKusalo khattadhammānaṃ tato pucchi anantarā Kacci bhoto kusalaṃ kacci bhoto anāmayaṃKacci raṭṭhamidaṃ phītaṃ dhammenamanusissati Kusalañceva me haṃsa atho haṃsa anāmayaṃAtho raṭṭhamidaṃ phītaṃ dhammenamanusissati Kacci bhoto amaccesu doso koci na vijjatiKaccinnu te tavatthesu nākaṅkhanti jīvitaṃ Atho pi me amaccesu doso koci na vijjatiAtho pi te mamatthesu nāvakaṅkhanti jīvitaṃ Kacci te sādisi bhariyā assavā piyabhāṇinīPuttarūpayasupetā mama chandavasānugā Atho me sādisi bhariyā assavā piyabhāṇinīPuttarūpayasupetā mama chandasānugā  Kacci raṭṭhaṃ anuppīḷaṃ akutoci upadadvaṃAsāhasena dhammena samena manusissati Ediso kho arahati  machasaṃ syā  Matthinnaṃ  machasaṃ vatthinaṃ  syā Samenamanusāsasi  machasaṃ      Atho raṭṭhaṃ anuppīḷaṃ akutoci upadadvaṃAsāhasena dhammena samena manusissati Kacci santo apacitā asanto parivajjitāNo ce dhammaṃ niraṅkatvā adhammamanuvattasi  Santo ca me apacitā asanto parivajjitāDhammamevānuvattāmi adhammo me niraṅkato Kacci nānāgataṃ dīghaṃ samavekkhasi khattiyaKacci na matto madaniye paralokaṃ na santatasi Nāhaṃ anāgataṃ dīghaṃ samavekkhāmi pakkhima ṭhito dasasu dhammesu paralokaṃna santase Dānaṃ sīlaṃ pariccāgaṃ ajjavaṃ maddavaṃ tapaṃAkkodhaṃ avihiṃsañca khantiñca avirodhanaṃ Iccete kusale dhamme ṭhite pasasāmi attaniTato me jāyate piti somanasasaññacanappakaṃ Sumukho ca acintetvā vissaji pharusaṃ giraṃBhāvadosamanaññāya asmākāyaṃ vihaṅgamo So kuddho pharusaṃ vācaṃ nicchachāresi ayonisoYānasmāsu na vijjanti na idaṃ paññavatāmiva  Atthi metaṃ atisāraṃ vegena manujādhipaDhataraṭṭhe ca baddhasmiṃ dukkhaṃ me vipulaṃ ahu Tvaṃ no pitāva puttānaṃ bhūtānaṃ dharaṇirivaAsmākaṃ adhipantānaṃ khamassu rājakuñajara Etaṃ te anumodāma yaṃ bhāvaṃ na niguhasiKhīlaṃ pahindasi pakkhī ujukosi vihaṅgama Manusissahaṃ  machasaṃ  Mavattasi  machasaṃ  Akodhaṃ  machasaṃ Atho  machasaṃ  Yānasmesu  machasaṃ  Yaṃ kiñci ratanaṃ atthi kāsirājanivesaneRajataṃ jātarūpañca muttā veḷuriyā bahu  Maṇayo saṅkhamuttañca vatthakaṃ haricandanaṃAjinaṃ dantabhaṇḍañca lohaṃ kālāyasaṃ bahuṃEtaṃ dadāmi vo vintaṃ isseraṃ vissajāmi vo Addhā apaphitā tyamhā sakkatā ca rathesabhaDhammesu vattamānānaṃ tvaṃ no ācariyo bhava me sannicayo ca atthiSukiccharūpaṃ catidaṃ parittaṃPatthodano nālamayaṃ duvinnaṃ Suriyuggamanaṃ  machasaṃ  Bhavanato  machasaṃ Neva kiṇāmi napi vikkiṇāmi tyādi imā ekavisati gāthāyo heṭṭhā vādasanipātekosiyajātakepi dissanti Imasmimpi ṭhāne āgatā aṭṭhakathācariyo pana naguttame girivaregandhamādaneti Ito paṭṭhāya sudhābhojana jātakaṃ dassesiti  Appambhā appakaṃ dajjā anumajjhato majjhakaṃBahumhā bahukaṃ dajjā adānaṃ nupapajjati Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya dehi dānāni bhuñja caAriyaṃ maggaṃ samārūha nekāsi labhate sukhaṃ  Moghañcassa hutaṃ hoti moghañcāpi samihitaṃAtithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ eko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya dehi dānāni bhuñja caAriyaṃ maggaṃ samārūha nekāsi labhate sukhaṃ Saccaṃ tassa hutaṃ hoti moghañcāpi samihitaṃAtithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ neko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya dehi dānāni bhuñja caAriyaṃ maggaṃ samārūha nekāsi labhate sukhaṃ Sarañca juhati yo so bahukāya caDoṇe tibbarutitthasmiṃ sīghasote mahāvahe Atracassa hutaṃ hoti atracassa samihitaṃAtithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ neko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya dehi dānāni bhuñja caAriyaṃ maggaṃ samārūha nekāsi labhate sukhaṃ  Balisaṃ hi so niggalati dīghasutataṃ sabbandhanaṃAtithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ eko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya dehi dānāni bhuñja caAriyaṃ maggaṃ samārūha nekāsi labhate sukhaṃ  Uḷāravaṇṇā vata brāhmaṇā imeAyañca vo sunakho kissa hetuUccāvacaṃ vaṇṇanibhaṃ vikubbatiAkkhātha no brahmaṇā kenu tumbhe  Cando ca suriyo ca ubho idhāgatāAyaṃ pana mātali devasārathiSakkohamasmi tidasānamindoEso ca kho pañcasikhoti vuccati Pāṇissarā mutiṅgā ca murajāḷambarāni caSuttamenaṃ pabodhenti paṭibuddho ca nandati  Ye kecime maccharino kadariyāParibhāsakā samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃIdheva nikkhippa sarīradehaṃKāyassa bhedā nirayaṃ vajanti Ye kecime suggatimāsasānāDhamme ṭhitā saṃyame saṃvibhāgeIdheva nikkhippa sarīradehaṃKāyassa bhedā sugatiṃ vajanti Tvaṃ no ñāti purimāsu jātisuSo macchari rosako pāpadhammoTaveva atthāya idhāgatambhāMā pāpadhammo nirayaṃ apattha Addhā hi maṃ vo hitakāmā yaṃ maṃ samanusāsathaSohaṃ tathā karissāmi sabbaṃ vuttaṃ hitesihi  Esāhamajjeva upāramāmiNa cāpahaṃ kiñci kareyya pāpaṃNa cāpi me kiñci adeyyamatthiNa pāci datvā udakampahaṃ pibe Evañca me dadato sabbakālaṃBhogā ime vāsava khiyissantiTato ahaṃ pabbajissāmi sakkaHitvāna kāmāni yathodhikāniti  Naguttame girivare gandhamādaneModanti tā devavarāhipālitāAthāgamā isivaro sabbalokaguSupupphitaṃ dumavarasākhamādiya  Suciṃ sugandhaṃ tidasehi sakkataṃPupphuttamaṃ amaravarehi sevitaṃAladdha maccehi vā dānavehi vāAññatra devehi tadārahaṃ hidaṃ Tato catasso kanakattacūpamāUṭṭhāya nāriyo pamadādhipā muniṃĀsā ca saddhā ca tato sirī hiriIccabravuṃ nārada devabrāhmaṇaṃ Sace anuddiṭṭhaṃ tayā mahāmuniPupphaṃ imaṃ pārichatassa brahmeDadāhi no sabbagati te ijjhatuTvampi no hohi yatheva vāsavo Taṃ yācamānābhisamekkha nāradoIccabravī saṅkalahaṃ udirayiNa mayhamatthatthi imehi kocinaṃYā yeva vo seyyasī sā piḷayhatha  Tvaṃ nottamovābhisamekkha nāradaYassicchasi tassaṃ anuppacecchasuYassā hi no nārada tvaṃ padassasiSā yeva no hohiti seṭṭhasammatā Akallametaṃ vacanaṃ sugatteKo brāhmaṇo ko kalahaṃ udirayeGantvāna bhūtādhipameva pucchathaSace na jānātha idhuttamādhamaṃ Tā nāradena parampapakopitāUdiritā vaṇṇamadena mattāSakāse ganatvāna sahassacakkhunoPucchiṃsu bhūtādhipaṃ kānu seyyasi  Tā disvā āyattamanā purandadoIccabravi devavaro katañajalīSabbāva vo hotha sugatte sādisiKo neva bhadde kalahaṃ udirayi Pilandhetha  vi Machasaṃ  Sakāsaṃ  machasaṃ  Yo sabbalokaṃ carako mahāmuniDhamme ṭhito nārado saccanikkamoSo no bravi girivare gandhamādaneGantvāna bhūtādhipameva pucchathaSace na jānātha idhuttamādhamaṃ Asu brahāraññacaro mahāmuniNādatvā bhattaṃ varagatte bhuñjaniViceyya dānāni dadāti kosiyoYassā hi so dassati sāva seyyasi  Asuhi yo sammati dakkhiṇaṃ disaṃGaṅgāya tīre himavantapasmanīSa kosiyo dullabhapānabhojanoTassa sudhaṃ pāpaya devasārathi Sa mātali devavarena pesitoSahassayuttaṃ abhiruyha sandanaṃSa khippameva upagamma assamaṃAdissamāno munino sudhaṃ adā Udaggihuttaṃ upatiṭṭhāto hi mePabhaṅkaraṃ lokatamonuduttamaṃSabbāni bhūtāni aticca vāsavoKo neva me pāṇisu kiṃ sudhodahi Saṃkhupamaṃ setamatulyadassanaṃSuciṃ sugandhaṃ piyarūpambhutaṃAdiṭṭhapubbaṃ mama jāta cakkhuhiKā devatā pāṇisu kiṃ sudhodahi  Ahaṃ mahindena mahesi pesitoSudhābhihāsiṃ turito mahāmuniJānāsi maṃ mātali deva sārathiBhuñjassu bhattuttamaṃ mā vicārayi Bhuttā ca sā dvādasa hanti pāpakeKhudaṃ pipāsaṃ aratiṃ daraklamaṃ Kodhupanāhañca vivādapesunaṃSītuṇhatandiñca rasuttamaṃ idaṃ Adāsi  machasaṃ  Jātu machasaṃ  Mātabhicārayi  machasaṃ Darathakkhamaṃ  machasaṃ durakkamaṃ  vi darathaṃ kīlaṃ  syā  Na kappati mātali mayha bhuñjituṃPubbe adatvā iti me vatuttamaṃNa cāpi ekāsanamariyapujitaṃAsaṃvibhāgi ca sukhaṃ na vindati Thighātakā yecime pāradārikāMittadduno yeca sapanti subbateSabbeva te maccharīpañca mādhamāTasmā adatvā udakampi nāsmiye  Yo hitthiyā cā purisassa vā panaDassāmi dānaṃ vidusampavaṇṇitaṃSaddhā vadaññu idha vitamaccharāBhavanti hete sucisammasammatā  Ato mutā devavarena pesitāKaññā catasso kanakattacūpamāĀsā ca saddhā ca sirī tato hiriTaṃ assamaṃ āgamuṃ yattha kosiyo Tā disvā sabbo paramappamoditoSubhena vaṇṇena sikhārivagginoKaññā catasso caturo catuddisāIccabravi mātalino ca sammukhā Purimaṃ disaṃ kā tvaṃ pabhāsi devateAlaṅkatā tāravarāva osadhiPucchāmi taṃ sabbakāmehi nāro pamodatiSiriti maṃ jānahi pujahatuttamaTaṃ maṃ sudhāya varapañña bhājaya Suvisacca  vi machasaṃ syā  Deva  machasaṃ Matā  machasaṃ syā  So  vi machasaṃ syā Devate  machasaṃ  Siritu vandalovaneNa bhāyasi ekikā kānane vane Na me dutiyo idhamatthi kosiyaMasakkasārappabhavambhi devatāĀsā sudhāsāya tavantimāgatāTaṃ maṃ sudhāya varapañña bhājaya  Āsāya yanti vāṇijā dhanesinoNāvaṃ samāruyha parenti aṇṇaveTe tatthasidanti athopi ekadāJinādhanā enti vinaṭṭhapābhatā Āsāya khettāni kasanti kassakāVapanti khijāni karontupāyasoĪtinipātena avuṭṭhitāya vāNa kiñci vindanti tato phalāgamaṃ Paṭimukka  machasaṃ  Athattakārāni karonti bhattusuĀsaṃ purakkhatvā narā sukhesinoTe bhatturatthā atigāḷhitā punaDisā panassanti aladdha kiñcanaṃ Jahitva  dhaññañca ñātakeĀsāya saggādhimanā Añajanamanosilābharitālahiṅgulakahemarajatakanakānekadhātusatavinaddhapatimaṇḍitappadese evarūpe khalu bhoramme vanasaṇḍe kuṇālo nāma sakuṇo paṭivasati ativiya citto ativiya cittapattacchadanoTasesva khalu bho kuṇālassa sakuṇassa aḍḍhuḍḍhāni itthisahassāni paricārikādijakaññāyo Atha khalu bho dve dijakaññayo kaṭṭhaṃ mukhena ḍasitvā taṃ kuṇālaṃsakuṇaṃ majjhe nisidāpetvā uḍḍenti mā naṃ kuṇālaṃ sakuṇaṃ addhānapariyāyapathekilamatho ubbāheyyāti pañcasatā dijakaññāyo heṭṭhato heṭṭhato ḍenti sacāyaṃ kuṇālosakuṇo āsanā paripaṭissati mayaṃ taṃ pakkhehi paṭiggahessāmāti Pañcasatā dijakaññāyouparūpari ḍenti mā naṃ kuṇālaṃ sakuṇaṃ ātapo paritāpiti Pañcasatā dijakaññāyo ubhatopassena ḍenti mā naṃ kuṇālaṃ sakuṇaṃ sītaṃ vā uṇhaṃ vā tiṇaṃ vā rajo vā vāto vā ussāvovā upappusiti Pañcasatā dijakaññāyo purato purato ḍenti mā naṃ kuṇālaṃ sakuṇaṃgopālakā vā pasupālakā vā tiṇahārakā vā kaṭṭhahārakā vā vanakammikā vā kaṭṭhena vākaṭhalāya vā pāṇinā vā pāsāṇena vā leḍaḍunā vā aṇḍena vā satthena vā sakkharāya vāpahāraṃ adaṃsu Māyaṃ kuṇālo sakuṇo gacchehi vā latāhi vā rukkhehi vā sākhāhi vāthambhehi vā pāsāṇehi vā balavantehi vā pakkhihi saṅgā mesiti Pañcasatā dijakaññāyopacchato pacchato ḍenti saṇhāhi sakhilāhi mañajuhi madhurāhi vā cāhi samudācarantiyomāyaṃ kuṇālo sakuṇo āsane pariyukkaṇṭhiti Pañcasatā dijakaññāyo diso disaṃ ḍentinekarukkhavividhavikatiphalamāharantiyo māyaṃ kuṇālo sakuṇo khudāya parilamitthātaatha khalu bho tā dijakaññāyo taṃ kuṇālaṃ sakuṇaṃ ārāmeneva ārāmaṃ uyyānenevauyyānaṃ naditittheneva nidatitthaṃ pabbatasikhareneva pabbatasikharaṃ ambavanenevaambavanaṃ jambuvaneneva jambuvanaṃ labujavaneneva labujavanaṃ nāḷikerasañcāriyenevanāḷikerasañcāriyaṃ khippameva abhisambhonti ratatthāya Atha khalu bho kuṇālo sakuṇotāhi dijakaññāhi divasaṃ paribbuḷho evaṃ apasādeti nassatha tumbhe vasaliyo vinassathatumbhe vasaliyo coriyo dhuttiyo asatiyo lahucitatāyo katassa appatikārikāyo anilo viya yenakāmaṅgamāyoti Ḍaṃsitvā  machasaṃ syā taṃpuṇṇamukhaṃphussakokilaṃ majjhe nisidāpetvā uḍḍeniti mā naṃ puṇṇamukhaṃphussakakokilaṃ addhānapariyāyapathe kilamatho ubbahetthāni Paññasa dijakaññāyoheṭṭhato yeṭṭhato ḍenti sacāyaṃ puṇṇamukho phussakokilo āsanā paripatissati mayaṃ taṃpakkhehi paṭiggahessāmāti Paññāya dija kaññāyo uparūpari ḍenti mā naṃ puṇṇamukhaṃphussakokilaṃ ātapo paritāpiti Paññasa dijakaññāyo ubhato passena ḍenti mā naṃpuṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ sītaṃ vā uṇhaṃ vā tiṇaṃ vā rajo vā vāto vā ussāvo vāupapphusiti Paññasa dijakaññāyo purato purato ḍenti mā naṃ puṇṇamukhaṃphussakokilaṃ gopālakā vā pasupālakā vā tiṇahārakā vā kaṭṭhahārakā vā vanakammikā vākaṭṭhena vā kaṭhalāya vā pāṇihārakā vā kaṭṭhahārakā vā vanakammikā vā kaṭṭhena vākaṭhalā vā pāṇinā vā pāsāṇena vā leḍaḍunā vā daṇḍena vā satthena vā sakkharāhi vā Kurāvaka  machasaṃ Pahāraṃ adaṃsu Māyaṃ puṇṇamukho phussakokilo gacchehi vā latāhi vā rukkhehi vāsākhāhi vā thambhehi vā pāsāṇehi vā balavantehi vā pakkhihi saṃgāmesīti Paññasadijakaññāyo pacchato pacchato ḍenti saṇhāhi sakhilāhi mañajuhi madhurāhi vācāhisamudācarantiyo māyaṃ puṇṇamukho phussakokilaṃ āsane pariyukkaṇṭhiti Paññasadijakaññāyo disodisaṃ ḍenti nekarukkhavividhavikatiphalamarahantiyo māyaṃpuṇṇamukho phussakokilo khudāya parikilamitthāti Atha khalu bho taṃ tā dijakaññāyotaṃ puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ ārāmeneva arāmaṃ uyyāneneva uyyānaṃ nadititthenevapabbatasikhareneva pabbatasikharaṃ ambavaneneva ambavana jambuvanaiva jambuvanaṃlabujavaneneva lakhujavanaṃ kāḷikerasañcāriyeneva nāḷikerasañcāriyaṃ khippamevaabhisambhonti atathoya Atha khalu bho puṇṇamukho phussakokilo tāhi dijakaññāhidivasaṃ paribbuḷho evaṃ pasaṃsati sādhu sādhu bhaginiyo etha kho bhaginiyo tumbhākaṃpatirūpaṃ kuladhitānaṃ yaṃ tumbhe bhattāraṃ paricareyyāthātiAtha khalu bho puṇṇamukho phussakokile yena kuṇālo sakuṇo tenupasaṅkamiAddasaṃsu kho kuṇālassa sakuṇassa paricārikā dijakaññāyo taṃ puṇṇamukhaṃphussakokilaṃduratova āgacchantaṃ disvāna yena puṇṇamukho phussakokilotenupasaṅkamiṃsu Upasaṅkamitvā taṃ puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ etadavocuṃ Ayaṃsammapuṇṇamukha kuṇālo sakuṇo ativiya pharuso atitiviyapharusavāco appevanāmatvampi āgamma piyavācaṃ labheyyāmāti Appevanāma bhaginiyoti vatvā yenakuṇālosakuṇo tenupasaṅkami upasaṅkamitvā kuṇālena sakuṇena saddhiṃ paṭisammoditvāekamantaṃ nisīdi Ekamantaṃ nisinno kho puṇṇamukho phussakokilo taṃ khuṇālaṃsakuṇaṃ etadavoca kissa tvaṃ smama kuṇāla itthinaṃ sujātānaṃ kuladhitānaṃ smamāpaṭipannānaṃ micchā paṭipantosi Amanāpabhāṇinampi kira samma kuṇāla itthinaṃmanāpabhāṇinā bhavitabbaṃ kimaṅgaṃ pana manāpabhāṇinanti Evaṃ apasādesi Tassatvaṃ samma jamma vasala vinassa tvaṃ smama jamma vasala konu tayā viyatto jāyājinenātiEvaṃ apasādito ca pana puṇṇamukho phussakokilo tato heva paṭinivatti Atha khalu bho puṇṇamukhassa phussakokilassa aparena samayena na cirasseva accayenakharo ābādho uppajja lohitapakkhandikā bāḷhā vedanā vattanti māraṇantikā Atha khalubho puṇṇamukhassa phussakokilassa paricārikānaṃ dijakaññānaṃ etadahosi Ābādhiko khoayaṃ puṇṇamukho phussakokilo appevanāma imambhā ābādhā vuṭṭhabheyyāti Taṃekakaṃ adutiyaṃ ohāya yena kuṇālo sakuṇo tenupasaṅkamiṃsu Addasā kho kuṇālosakuṇo tā dijakaññāyo duratova āgacchantiyo dinvāna tā dijakaññāyo etadavo kahaṃ panatumbhaṃ vasaliyo bhattāni Ābādhiko kho samma kuṇāla puṇṇamukho phusasakokiloappevanāma tambhā ābādhā vuṭṭhaheyyāti Evaṃ vutte kuṇālo sakuṇo tā dijakaññāyo evaṃapasādesi Nassatha tumbhe vasaliyo vinassatha tumebha vasaliyo coriyo dhuttiyo asatiyolahuvitatāyo katassa apaṭikārikāyo anilo viya yena kāmaṅgamāyoti Vatvā yenapuṇṇamukho phussakokilo tenupasaṅkami upasaṅkamitvā ta puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃetadavoca haṃ samma puṇṇamukhāti haṃ samma kuṇālāti atha khalu bho kuṇālosakuṇo taṃ puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ pakkhehi ca mukhatuṇḍena ca pariggahetvāvuṭṭhāpetvā nānābhesajjāni pāyāpesi Atha khalu bho puṇṇamukhassa phussakokilassa soabādho paṭippassambhitiAtha khalu bho kuṇālo sakuṇo taṃ puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ gilānā vuṭṭhitaṃaciravuṭṭitaṃ gelaññā etadavoca Diṭṭhā māya sammā puṇṇamukha kanhādvepitikāpañcapatikāya chaṭṭhe purise cittaṃ paṭibaddhantiyā yadidaṃ kavandhepiṭhasappiyabhiti Bhavati ca panuttarettha vākyaṃ  Pathajjuno nakulo bhimasenoYudhiṭṭhilo saha devoca rājāEte pati pañcamaticca nārīAkāsi khujjavāmanakena pāpantiDiṭṭhā mayā samma puṇṇamukha kuruṅgadevināma lomasundari eḷakamārakaṃ kāmayamānā chaḷaṅgakumāradhananetavāsināpāpamakāsi Evaṃ hetaṃ mayā ñātaṃ brahmadattassa mātaraṃObhāya kosalarājaṃ pañcālacaṇḍena pāpamakāsa Etā ca aññā ca me na purenti te me suṇātha bhāsato Samuddo brāhmaṇo rājā itthi cāpi dijampati Saritā sāgaraṃ yanti yā kāci paṭhiviṃsitā Tā samuddaṃ na purenti ūnattā hi na purati Brāhmaṇo ca adhiyāna vedamakkhānapañcamaṃBhiyyopi sutamiccheyya ūnattā hi na purati Rājā ca paṭhaviṃ sabbaṃ sasamuddaṃ sapabbataṃAjjhāvasaṃ vijinitvā anantaratanocitaṃPāraṃ samuddaṃ pattheti ūnattā hi na purati Evamekāya itthiyā aṭṭhaṭṭha patino siyāSurā ca balavantā ca sabbakāmarasāharāKāreyya navame chandaṃ ūnattā hi na purati Sabbitthiyo sikhiriva sabbabhakkhāSabbitthiyo nadiriva sabbavāhini Sabbitthiyo kaṇṭakānaṃ caranti pamadāhanatthikā  Kuṇālo haṃ tadā āsiṃ udiyi phussakokiloĀnando gijjharājāsi sāriputto ca nāradoParisā buddhaparisā evaṃ dhāretha jātakanti Kuṇālajātakaṃ Osajitvā  machasaṃ  Nayissati Passasi  machasaṃ passeyya  syā passeti  vi  Sake te raṭṭhe  machasaṃ  Chiddante raṭṭhaṃ byadhitaṃ bhayāhiPuthu narā leṇamanuppaviṭṭhāManussamaṃsaṃ viramehi rājaEtaṃ varānaṃ catutthaṃ varāmi  Addhā hi so bhakkho mamaṃ manāpoEtassa hetumhi vanaṃ paviṭṭhoSohaṃ kathaṃ etto upārameyyaṃAññaṃ varānaṃ catutthaṃ varassu Na ce piyaṃ meti janinda tādisoAttaṃ niraṃkatvā piyāni sevati attāva soyyo paramāva aseyyoLabbhā piyā ocitatthena pacchā  Piyaṃ me mānusaṃ maṃsaṃ sutasoma vijānahiNambhi sakko nivāretuṃ aññaṃ tuvaṃ samma varaṃ varassu Yo ve piyaṃ meti piyānukaṅkhiAttaṃ niraṃ katvā piyāni sevatiSoṇḍāva pitvāna visassa thālaṃTeneva so hoti dukhi parattha Yo cīdha saṅkhāya piyāni hitvāKicchenapi sevati ariyadhammaṃDukkhitova pītvāna yathosadhāniTeneva so hoti sukhī parattha Ohāyahaṃ pitaraṃ mātarañcaManāpike kāmaguṇe ca pañcaEtassa hetumbhi vanaṃ paviṭṭhoTante varaṃ kinti mahaṃ dadāmi  Na paṇḍitā dviguṇaṃ ahu vākyaṃSaccappaṭiññāva bhavanti santoVarassu samma iti maṃ avocaIccabravi tvaṃ na hi te sameti Apuññalābhaṃ ayasaṃ akittiṃPāpaṃ bahuṃ duccaritaṃ kilesaṃManussamaṃsassa kate upāgāTante varaṃ kintimahaṃ dadeyyaṃ Nahisakkā  machasaṃ  Aariyadhamme  vi machasaṃ syā Piyānurakkhi  machasaṃ syā  Manāpiye  machasaṃ Visamissa  vi machasaṃ syā  Bhavo  machasaṃ Dukkhi  machasaṃ syā  Na taṃ varaṃ arahati jantu dātuṃYaṃ vāpi datvāna avākareyyaVarassu samma avikampamānoPāṇaṃ cajitvānapi dassameva Pāṇaṃ cajanti santo nāpi dhammaṃSaccappaṭiññā ca bhavanti santoDatvā varaṃ khippamavākarohiEtena sampajja surājaseṭṭha  Dhanaṃ caje yo pana aṅgahetuAṅgaṃ caje jīvitaṃ jakkhamānoAṅga dhanaṃ jīvitaṃ cāpi sabbaṃCaje naro dhammamanussaranto Yassā hi dhammaṃ puriso vijaññāYe cassa kaṅkhaṃ vinayanti santoTaṃ hissa dipañca parāyaṇañcaNa tena mittiṃ jarayetha pañño  Addhā hi so bhakakho mamaṃ manāpoEtassa hetumbhi vanaṃ paviṭṭhoSaceva maṃ yācasi etamatthaṃEtampi te samma varaṃ dadāmi  Satthā ca me hosi sakhā ca mesiVacanampi te samma ahaṃ akāsiṃTuvampi me samma karohi vākyaṃUbhopi gantvāna pamocayāma Satthā ca te homi sakhā ca tyambhiVacanampi me samma ahaṃ akāsiAhampi te samma karomi vākyaṃUbhopi gantvāna pamocayāma Kammāsapādena viheṭhitatthaTalāvutā assumukhā rudantāNa jātu dubbhetha imassa raññoSaccappaṭiññaṃ me paṭissuṇātha Cajedhanaṃ aṅgavarassahetu  vi machasaṃ syā  Jirayetha  machasaṃ  Mama machasaṃ  Vihedhitambhā  machasaṃ syā  Kammāsapādena viheṭhitambhāTalāvutā assumukhā rudantāNa jātu dubbhetha imassa raññoSaccappaṭiññante paṭissuṇāma  Yathā pitā vā athavāpi mātāAnukampakā atthakāmā pajānaṃEvameva vo hotu ayañca rājāTumbhe ca vo hotha yatheva puttā Yathā pitā vā athavāpi mātāAnukampakā atthakāmā pajānaṃEvameva no hotu ayañca rājāMayampi bhessāma yatheva puttā Catuppadaṃ sakuṇañcāpi maṃsaṃSudehi randhaṃ sukataṃ suniṭṭhitaṃSudhaṃva indo paribhuñajiyānaHitvā katheko ramasi araññe   Tā khattiyā velali vilākamajjhāAlaṅkatā samparivārayitvāIndaṃva devesu pamodayiṃsuHitvā katheko ramasi araññe Tambupadhāne bahugoṇakambhiSucimbhi sabbassayanambhi saññate Sayanassa majjhambhi sukhaṃ sayitvāHitvā katheko ramasi araññe Pāṇissaraṃ kumbhathunaṃ nisitheAthopi ve nippurisampi turiyaṃBahuṃ sugitañca suvāditañcaHitvā katheko ramasi araññe Uyyānasampannaṃ pahutamālyaṃMigāvirūpena puraṃ surammaṃHayehi nāgehi rathehupetaṃHitvā katheko ramasi araññe Valli  machasaṃ  Subhamabhisabbasasayanambhi saṅgate  machasaṃ syā Seyyassa  machasaṃ  Niside  machasaṃ syā  Bahutta  machasaṃ Migājinupeta  syā   Kāḷapakkhe yathā cando hāyateva suve suveKāḷapakkhupamo rāja asataṃ hoti samāgamo Yathā rasakamāgamma sudakaṃ purisādhamaṃAkāsiṃ pāpakaṃ kammaṃ yena gacchāmi duggatiṃ Sukkapakkhe yathā cando vaḍḍhateva suve suveSukkapakkhupamo rāja sataṃ hoti samāgamo Yathāhaṃ tava māgamma sutasoma vijānahiKāhāmi kusalaṃ kammaṃ yena gacchāmi suggatiṃ  Thale yathā vāri janinda vaṭṭaṃAnaddha neyyaṃ aciraṭṭhitikaṃEvampi ce hoti asataṃ samāgamoAnadadhaneyyo udakaṃ thaleva Sare yathā vāri jinindaṃ vaṭṭaṃCiraṭṭhitikaṃ naraviriya seṭṭhaEvampi ve hoti sataṃ samāgamo Avyāyiko hoti sataṃ samāgamoYāvampi tiṭṭheyya tatheva hotiKhippaṃ hi veti asataṃ samāgamoTasmā sataṃ dhammo asabbhi ārakā  Na so rājā yo ajeyyaṃ jinātiNa so sakhā yo sakhāraṃ jinātiNa sā bhariyā yā patito vibhetiNa te puttā ye na bharanti jiṇṇaṃ Na sā sabhā yattha na santi santoSanto na te ye na bhananti dhammaṃRāgañca dosañca pahāya mohaṃDhammaṃ bhaṇantova bhananti santo Vuṭṭhaṃ  machasaṃ  Ananda  machasaṃ  Naravira  machasaṃ Ciraṭṭhitika  machasaṃ  Rājā naso yo  machasaṃ  Puttā  nate ye  machasaṃ  Na bhāsamānaṃ jānanti missaṃ bālehi paṇḍitaṃBhāsamānañca jānanti desentaṃ amataṃ padaṃ Bhāsaye jotaye dhammaṃ paggaṇhe isinaṃ dhajaṃSubhāsitaddhajā isayo dhammo hi isinaṃ dhajotiMahāsutasomajātakaṃAsitinipāto niṭṭhitoTassuddānaṃSumukho pana haṃsavaro ca mahāSudhābhojanino ca paro pavaroSakuṇāladijādhipativabhayanoSutasoma varuttama samhayanoti Nābhāsa  machasaṃ  Subhāsita
